Current Commentary

The King of Yugoslavia Assassinated Heng 17

Twenty years ago, the Austrian Crown Prince toured the south and was killed by a Serbian assassin, which led to the Great War in Europe. Since that war, this small Serbia has merged with the formerly Austro-Hungarian-controlled Croats and Slovenes to form Yugoslavia. Unexpectedly, twenty years later, the King of Yugoslavia has again died at the hands of a Croat. At this time of international turmoil, it is truly a feeling of "rare coincidence." The previous tragedy occurred because the Serbian people of the provinces of Bosnia and Herzegovina were under Austro-Hungarian rule, hindering the Serbian people's Greater Serbia ideology. The latter tragedy occurred because the Croats, under the mixed rule of the three Yugoslav groups, were unable to develop their independent actions. Therefore, although the time and place of their occurrence are different, their nature is quite similar.

However, although their nature is similar, there are also differences. The Serbs and Austro-Hungarians are of completely different ethnicities, and naturally, they were unwilling to be ruled by foreigners. This is one difference. Although Serbia's territory was small at that time, it was still an independent country. Since the Austrian Crown Prince died at the hands of a Serb, Austria had the necessity to declare war on Serbia. This is not the case with the Croats today. First, they are not an independent country, and second, they belong to the same Slavic race as the Serbian people and are still one of the Yugoslav ethnic groups. Therefore, this tragedy is purely an internal problem of Yugoslavia, and the results it produces will be different from the previous war.

Why is this tragedy an internal problem of Yugoslavia? This is not difficult to understand. Although today's Yugoslavia is an expansion of the former Serbia, its ethnic groups all belong to the Slavic family. However, based on differences in language, customs, religion, and civilization, excluding a few ethnic minorities, it can be divided into three major groups: the Serbs, who account for about seven million; the Croats, who account for about three million; and the Slovenes, who account for about one and a half million, plus two and a half million from smaller ethnic groups, for a total of fourteen million people. The Serbs mostly belong to the Greek Orthodox religion, and the alphabet they use is also different from that of the Croats. In terms of culture, the Serbs are mostly farmers and have Eastern ethnic characteristics. However, the Croats and Slovenes have long been under Austro-Hungarian rule and are more advanced than the Serbs in terms of culture and industry. They belong to the Catholic Church. However, during the Great War, the three groups shared a sense of adversity and knew that without joining forces to unite and form a common country, it would be insufficient to cope with future difficulties. Therefore, the Corfu Declaration was established in 1917, which became the initial charter for the founding of Yugoslavia. However, among the three groups, the Serbs were the most numerous, so the Serbs took the advantage in politics. Therefore, they used their political power everywhere to continue their pre-war Greater Serbia ideal. However, from the perspective of the Croats, this policy actually made them regress and gradually orientalize. Therefore, they gradually felt that it was a miscalculation to merge with Serbia in the first place. In 1919, the Croats once organized a Croatian Republic, which was quickly destroyed and did not last long, but the movement for separation and independence never waned. By 1923, the Croats had another attempt to organize a country, but it also failed. Later, although the Croats often tried to win in the parliament, the results were few. After the assassination of Croatian political leader Radić in 1928, King Alexander of Yugoslavia abolished the constitution, banned party activities, and took over the power to implement a policy of assimilation of Croat and Slovene regions. This fundamentally struck a blow to the Croats' separation and independence movement. In 1931, Alexander promulgated the Royal Constitution. Although the upper and lower houses were established, half of the upper house members were appointed by the king, and half were elected by the people. The lower house members were elected from a list prepared by the government. Therefore, it was difficult for the representatives of the Croats to win in both houses. This is the reason why the Croats resented Alexander. Therefore, the background of the death of the King of Yugoslavia this time is purely internal.

However, recent developments in the international situation have also contributed to the rapid outbreak of this tragedy. In order to achieve their separation and independence, the Croats were unwilling to see Yugoslavia's international status become more secure. However, since this spring, first, the signing of the Balkan Pact has greatly stabilized Yugoslavia's position in the Balkans. In March and September of this year, Alexander visited Bulgaria twice, which dissolved the long-standing feud between the two countries. Recently, due to France's mediation, Italy's attitude towards Yugoslavia will also be greatly improved. All of these are sufficient to strengthen the unification of Yugoslavia and facilitate the Serbs' assimilation policy. It is reasonable for the Croats to value the King of Yugoslavia's visit to France this time and believe that it is the key to the fate of the Croats in the future. Therefore, there is no doubt that the assassin's actions were purely politically motivated.

As for the impact of this incident on the international situation, it can also be said.

(1) According to the observations of some European diplomatic representatives stationed in Washington, D.C., the Croats may take advantage of this change to seek to break away from Serbia or demand a high degree of autonomy. The result may cause serious international disputes. Most Italians and Croatian nationalists express sympathy, while France advocates that the Croatian nation should unite with the Serbs.

(2) The death of the King of Yugoslavia may affect the future London Naval Conference. The coordination of France and Italy is a prerequisite for the smooth progress of the naval conference, and Alexander has always opposed it. Italy's policy in the Adriatic Sea conflicts with the interests of Yugoslavia. Disputes have continued since the war. Yugoslavia, Czechoslovakia, and Romania, commonly known as the Little Entente, are under the Versailles system with France and Belgium. The French secretly regard themselves as their protectors. Since the French want to coordinate with Italy, they must first eliminate Yugoslavia's backlash in order to win the favor of the Little Entente countries. Barthou has been running around, traveling between Barlette and Rome. The biggest mission is to reach an understanding before Mussolini's speech in Milan. He has expressed his willingness to peacefully resolve the conflict with the South and is particularly satisfied with the close relationship with France. Now that the King of Yugoslavia and Barthou have unfortunately died at the same time, the relationship between France, Italy, and the South will inevitably be greatly affected. Moreover, the balance of power in the Balkans has been shaken as a result, and major changes have taken place in the Mediterranean situation. The British may pay special attention to this matter, and it is not impossible to build more warships to monitor the Italians. If Britain and Italy compete to build warships, the United States, France, and Japan will hardly sit idly by. As a result, it will not only run counter to the purpose of naval disarmament.

(3) Italy has repeatedly declared that it will do its best to maintain the independence and integrity of Austria in order to prevent the Vienna government from becoming friendly with the German National Socialist Party. Yugoslavia was originally a part of the old Austro-Hungarian Empire. Because Austria has a movement to revise the Treaty of Trianon, it is deeply afraid that once it becomes a reality, it will be unfavorable to its own country. Therefore, it wants to unite with Germany to contain Austria and resist Italy. In May of this year, German government Aviation Minister and Prussian Prime Minister General Göring personally visited Nanjing and publicly declared that Yugoslavia was a major power in the Balkan Peninsula, which was disliked by Austria and Italy. The diplomatic community also regards Göring's actions as another proof of the close friendship between Germany and Yugoslavia to resist Italy's policy in Central Europe, which may not be an overstatement. Now that the King of Yugoslavia has died prematurely and the Crown Prince has ascended the throne at a young age, it would be fortunate enough to maintain domestic peace. It is feared that it will be difficult to continue his father's legacy, unite with Germany to resist Italy. What can be predicted is that, according to the recent declaration of the French government, France will pay more attention to Yugoslavia's national policy in the future. In times of crisis, it will not hesitate to provide substantial assistance. Moreover, the Queen of Alexander is a Romanian princess. The two countries can help each other due to their marriage and alliance relationship in order to maintain this extraordinary situation and keep the young master in his position. If there is no internal strife in Yugoslavia, the international disputes on the surface may not be difficult to eliminate.

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek Issues Another Order to Ban Opium in Various Provinces 18

(Nanchang) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek recently telegraphed the governments of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Jiangxi, Hunan, Shaanxi, and Gansu provinces, ordering them to ban the cultivation of opium. The telegram stated, "Opium has been poisoning our country for decades. The reason why it has not been eradicated is that the government lacks strict and unified control measures and there are no consistent and effective steps. The practice of tolerating and accommodating has led to the increasing cultivation of poppies. Even in provinces and regions that did not previously cultivate opium, they gradually disregard the laws and secretly cultivate opium. As the production of opium increases, so does the number of people addicted to it. This chairman deeply knows that to eliminate the scourge of opium and eradicate the poisonous atmosphere, it is necessary to start with banning cultivation in order to achieve a thorough cleansing effect. Previously, the bandit suppression headquarters of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui provinces issued measures for assigning personnel to investigate and ban opium cultivation in ten provinces, as well as precautions for investigating and banning opium cultivation. If the provinces can earnestly follow and advance in an orderly manner, it would not be difficult to gradually eradicate opium. However, in remote counties and remote areas of the provinces where opium was banned last year, according to investigations, there is still much secret cultivation, which is extremely distressing. It must be known that whether the opium ban can be implemented is greatly related to the rise and fall of the nation and international credibility. Local officials must not be allowed to continue to condone and tolerate this. Now, I am issuing the previous order again, urging you to earnestly abide by the previous opium ban measures and the precautions for banning cultivation, and to strictly prohibit sowing within the year 23 of the Republic of China, so as to eliminate poisonous plants together. Next year, no opium seedlings are allowed to emerge. This headquarters will not temporarily appoint supervisors, but will send secret investigators to conduct strict inspections anytime and anywhere, take photos, and secretly report. All supervisory tasks are completely entrusted to the provincial governments to earnestly implement, strictly order the counties to obtain guarantees from each township that opium will never be cultivated, and the county magistrate should add a ban on cultivation seal, which will be submitted to the provincial government for verification. When necessary, personnel will be sent to conduct general inspections. If any opium seedlings are found in the counties that have reported that opium cultivation has been banned and opium seedlings have been eradicated, the county magistrate, the investigators, and the gentry and planting households who have provided guarantees will all be severely punished in accordance with military law, without any leniency. If there is any military garrison protecting opium cultivation, the local administrative supervisor or county magistrate may directly telegraph this headquarters for verification. In addition to sending telegrams separately, I am urgently ordering the provincial government to comply with and forward to all subordinates to strictly abide by and report the compliance situation at any time for verification. Chiang Kai-shek's seal." (Central News Agency, 11th)

New Regulations on Local Administration in the Mausoleum Area 19

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior asked whether the local administration of the Mausoleum Area should be handled by the Mausoleum Management Committee, or should it still be managed by Jiangning County. Whether the autonomous region should be established as a special case, as an area between the county and the township, or should it be set up as a special autonomous experimental area, not subject to the current autonomous laws and regulations. What is the status of the administrative region and which administrative region is it equal to. In addition to issuing documents to ordinary provincial and municipal governments, should all laws and regulations promulgated by the Central Government be issued to the Mausoleum Management Committee at the same time. Is the Committee a central agency or a local agency? What should be the relationship between the various departments of the Central Government and the various local governments and the Mausoleum Management Committee? How should its powers and scope be defined? The government has no clear regulations. Please the Executive Yuan to submit to the Central Government for clear regulations on the above points in the regulations of the Mausoleum Management Committee. Subsequently, the Central Political Conference resolved that: 1. Judicial matters in the Mausoleum Area shall be handled by the Jiangning District Court. 2. The household registration of tenants and workers in the Mausoleum shall be handled by the Mausoleum Management Committee in conjunction with the Nanjing Municipal Government in the designated areas of Nanjing City for registration and elections. The above matters were communicated to the Civil Service Office of the National Government on the 11th and forwarded for compliance. (Special dispatch on the 11th)

Restrictions on the Import of Acetic Anhydride and Other Items and Related Issues 20

(Nanjing) Representatives from the League of Nations Opium Suppression Committee, the United States, and Spain stated that the large amount of caffeine and acetic anhydride imported into China in recent years is clear evidence of the manufacture of huge quantities of heroin. Our representative Hu Shi-ze suggested that customs list these items in a special clause and limit their import volume. The Ministry of Finance stated that acetic anhydride, in addition to being used in conjunction with heroin, can also be used to manufacture various non-toxic drugs, chemicals, neutral pigments, and wood acetate materials. As for caffeine, in addition to being used with lactose or narcotics to prepare red pills, it can also be used in conjunction with non-toxic drugs. If these two items are completely controlled, the legitimate businesses that use them to prepare other items will inevitably be damaged. Even if restrictions are imposed, these items may still be manufactured domestically. Unscrupulous merchants can still use them to manufacture heroin, so prevention is still ineffective. As for listing in a special clause for statistics, this can be done. The Standing Committee of the Opium Suppression Committee decided to postpone the restriction on caffeine and acetic anhydride until clear statistics are available. (Special dispatch on the 11th)

(Nanjing) The organization law of the preparatory committee for the Wenxi Paper Mill was approved by the Executive Yuan meeting last week and will be announced by the Ministry of Industry on the 12th. (Special dispatch on the 11th)

The Yellow River Is Pouring Down Vigorously from the Breach at Changyuan 24

(Jinan) At the Yellow River breach in Changyuan, the water is pouring down vigorously. The water level in the Jin Dike River on the north bank of the Yellow River in this province has risen sharply by 1.7 meters and is still rising. The water is more than ten li wide. Newly planted wheat seedlings in five counties, including Pu, Fan, Shou, Zhang, Yanggu, and Dong'e, have been completely submerged, and the disaster is as severe as last year. If the Changyuan breach is not blocked quickly, it will become more and more serious. In addition, the people's dike of the Yellow River in Feicheng has also been breached by more than 30 feet, flooding a lot of land. It is being rushed to be blocked. (Special dispatch on the 11th)

The Confucius Temple in Qufu Will Be Repaired Soon 25

The Central Government Remits 100,000 Yuan to Jinan

(Jinan) The Central Government has remitted 100,000 yuan to repair the Confucius Temple in Qufu. The remaining 100,000 yuan and the 50,000 yuan donated by Chiang Kai-shek will arrive soon. The provincial government will hold a meeting on the 12th to prepare for the start of construction. Dai Chuanxian advocated establishing a national primary and secondary school and academy in Qufu and will also inspect Qufu. (Special dispatch on the 11th)

Intelligence on Bandit Suppression in Various Areas 26

(Fuzhou) A telegram from [] to Fujian stated that the remnant bandits of Fang and Luo fled to Baojia Village and were pursued by our division. The bandits resisted stubbornly at Jinyin Mountain and Songfu Ridge. The battle was extremely fierce. Fortunately, the officers and soldiers charged bravely more than ten times, and the bandits died and were wounded in piles before they fled in a panic. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Xiamen) Headquarters News: The [] team advanced to Hubobei, five li east of Hetian, on the 6th. The bandits did not fight and abandoned all of Hetian and retreated west. We immediately occupied the nearby high mountains and built fortifications. Hetian is under the mountain and has become an empty town. We also did not garrison there, but crossed it with a part of our forces and gradually advanced westward. Although Hetian is important, it is not dangerous. Therefore, when the Nanshan Dam in the second line was breached, the bandits abandoned it without defending it. We also did not pay much attention to it. It is now 40 li away from Ting, all of which is flat land without high mountains. According to reports, the bandits also have the intention of abandoning Ting and retreating west without fighting. The capture of Ting is expected to be without much fighting and is very close, even during the day. Now that Shicheng has fallen and Changting is undefended, the bandits may abandon the Jiangxi-Fujian border altogether. (Special dispatch on the 11th)

(Nanchang) Zhai Jianmin, the regimental commander of the pseudo-13th Division, 38th Regiment, came over and confessed the situation of the bandit soldiers fleeing. The bandits are now using hundreds of thousands of our troops to encircle and attack them, so they are trying their best to expand the Red Army and implement the so-called mobilization work, conscripting able-bodied men for replenishment. However, the general public is suffering too much from the bandit army, without clothes or food, so they are taking the opportunity to flee. Each regiment has more than a hundred people deserting in a month. In Luokou before, there were many bandit soldiers who deserted. Most of the bandit soldiers of the pseudo-5th Army Corps were from Luokou. After the bandit soldiers deserted and returned home, the whole family had to flee, because they were afraid that the bandit government would find out and kill the whole family. Previously, when our army was about to pursue them to Luokou, the bandit soldiers who deserted and the refugees organized a desertion group of thousands of people and fled to our side. Now, the old soldiers of the bandit side (those who enlisted in February of this year) are their cadres. The new soldiers have no training and are only taught to load and unload bullets before going into battle. The officers monitor the soldiers extremely strictly, and the officers themselves and the soldiers are monitored by political commissars. If they hesitate at all, their lives are in danger. Every step they take is also monitored by their so-called resolute elements. Each company and battalion has resolute elements secretly mixed in, so the general psychology is one of terror all day long. (Central News Agency, 11th)

(Nanchang) Bai Chongxi's winter telegram: After Xiao bandits were defeated by our army on the 25th, they attempted to cross Huangqiao and flee northeast. They were intercepted by two battalions of our forces. Being in a very desperate situation, they fled to Bagua River. I sent two regiments to suppress them there on the morning of the 26th. The bandits were frightened and, after a brief encounter, fled to Daqing. The two regiments continued to pursue them closely, and the bandits were forced to flee north through Xiafengxi and Liang Kou to join He bandits. I have sent a large army to continue the fierce pursuit, and have telegraphed the Guizhou army to prepare for interception, and the Zhenyuan troops to block the river, in order to annihilate them. The investigation of the bandits in the area south of the Zhenyuan River revealed that the bandits had been fiercely pursued by our army for two days at Bagua River. The bandits abandoned many wounded bandits and luggage along the way, which was shocking to see. Their embarrassment had reached its limit, and there were also scattered bandits hiding in the mountains. When our army arrived, many of them immediately surrendered with weapons. The bandits were all skin and bones, which shows that the bandit's combat power is weak. If they are severely attacked once or twice again, they can be eliminated. In addition, the bandits left in Fengxi, about two to three thousand, first fled to Daqing and were severely attacked by our division, killing three to four hundred bandits, etc. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Nanchang) The headquarters announced that Liang's advance team of the Sixth Route Army launched a fierce attack with infantry and artillery on the 8th and 9th, defeating the pseudo-21st and 23rd divisions, and occupied the bandit positions and fortifications of Taiyang Peak in Xingguo. The bandit nest of Gulonggang is now under our control and is only ten li away. After we occupy the fortifications of each line, we will go straight to Gulonggang. (Special dispatch on the 11th)

(Nanjing) In order to promote export trade, the Ministry of Finance has granted a reduction of 2.5% in export tax on frozen duck, which is included in the fresh and frozen meat category of the current export tariff regulations, in accordance with the example of export tax reduction for eggs. The tax will be temporarily levied at 5% ad valorem, from October 1 of this year to the end of January next year, as a trial period. The Executive Yuan has forwarded it to the Ministry of Finance for notification. (Central News Agency, 11th)

The Ministry of Railways Requests the Abolition of the Actions of Inspection Personnel Along the Railway Line 36

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Railways recently stated that the inspection personnel along the railway line often do not follow the regulations and conduct inspections while the train is in motion, which affects public transportation and may even cause traffic accidents and serious dangers. It also stated that each railway itself has strict prevention and control measures for the investigation of smuggled goods and contraband. If any are found in transit, the people and goods will be sent to the local authorities for punishment according to law. Recently, the various inspection agencies have not fully understood the responsibilities and handling of the railways. The Ministry of Railways specially submitted a request to the Executive Yuan on the 11th, which was forwarded to the National Government, to issue a notice to all military and political agencies that all inspection personnel should abide by the road regulations and maintain the established practices, and it is prohibited to enter stations and conduct inspections in transit. Yugoslavia's King's Visit to France Ends in Assassination in Marseille 41

The Assassin is of Croatian Descent

French Foreign Minister Barthou Also Dies

Marseille – Yugoslavian King Alexander and French Foreign Minister Barthou were assassinated by a Croatian merchant this afternoon. This was King Alexander's first official visit to France after the European War. He was killed just minutes after arriving, causing a great shock to the diplomatic world. The King was assassinated at 4:10 PM this afternoon. The King and French Foreign Minister Barthou were riding in the same car when, upon reaching the stock exchange, a Croatian man named Karimen suddenly emerged from the crowd, jumped onto the car's fender, and fired a pistol through the window at the occupants. The King was hit by three bullets and immediately collapsed, bleeding from the mouth and chest. Barthou was hit in the abdomen and left arm. After the assassination, the perpetrator attempted to commit suicide with the gun, but was stopped by police. As they were about to take him into custody, the enraged crowd seized him and beat him to death on the spot.

King Alexander died minutes after being shot, the bullets piercing his chest. French Foreign Minister Barthou died at 5:40 PM, the bullet lodged deep in his abdomen. He was already unconscious when surgery was performed and could not be saved. After being shot, the King was taken to the police chief's office in the county government. Despite all efforts to save him, he could not be revived and died within minutes. (Reuters, 9th)

Belgrade – News of the assassination of King Alexander and French Foreign Minister Barthou was not initially announced. It was not until this morning that the government released an official statement, saying that it was deeply aware of the difficult situation and was taking steps to ensure national stability. A subsequent statement said that although the Yugoslavian people were saddened by the death of their monarch, the public was calm and the country was peaceful. (Reuters, 10th)

Amidst Welcoming Cheers, Yugoslavian King Suddenly Assassinated 42

Struck by Four Bullets, Dies Instantly

Barthou Also Sacrificed

Assassin of Southern Descent Killed on the Spot

Marseille – King Alexander I of Yugoslavia was riding in a car through the main streets of Marseille at 4:00 PM today, amidst welcoming cheers from the crowd, when he was assassinated by his political enemies exiled in France. Five others also died, including French Foreign Minister Barthou, who attempted to shield the French dignitary with his own body and was also sacrificed. This event is the most shocking since the assassination in Serbia. Other deceased include General George, a French military officer in the King's entourage, Count Jevtic, a court minister of the Southern Kingdom, an adjutant to the Southern King, and a French police officer. Five others were seriously injured, including French Admiral Bedreau. Queen Marie, who was traveling to Paris separately by train, fortunately escaped unharmed.

Last night, police announced that at least two people from the Southern Kingdom were involved in the assassination. The gunman who killed the King and Barthou was a 40-year-old merchant named Kilmen, who was killed by police and trampled by the crowd. The identity of the other person is not yet confirmed and is currently in police custody. It is reported that Kilmen is a Croat and belongs to a secret political party that vowed to kill the King because his autocratic policies were destroying Croatian autonomy. The tragedy occurred just minutes after the King arrived and began his motorcade. Marseille was warmly welcoming the monarch of a friendly nation, with warships lining the port, the French flagship firing salutes, and thousands of troops lining the coast and main roads. Military music filled the air as the King passed by, and French flags fluttered. Foreign Minister Barthou formally welcomed the King upon his arrival, and the King shook hands with everyone. Shortly after boarding the car, which was surrounded by many secret agents for protection, the King sat with Barthou and Count Jevtic, while General George sat on a folding chair and the adjutant sat next to the driver. The King's car was the fourth in the motorcade and slowly moved forward, reaching Cannabiere Street, where about 20,000 spectators lined the street, cheering and eager to catch a glimpse of the King. The King smiled and nodded, and occasionally saluted. The car was moving very slowly, and before it had gone a hundred feet from the port, Kilmen broke free from the police and jumped onto the running board of the car, immediately firing a pistol directly at the King, continuing to shoot until he was stabbed in a vital spot by the police. He did not think of escaping, clearly having decided to risk his life. The King was shot four times, and without saying a word, collapsed in the car, spitting blood from his mouth. Barthou was wounded in the arm by the first shot, but still jumped forward, trying to shield the dignitary, placing himself in front of the gunman's weapon. However, Kilmen pushed him away, and Barthou fell. The driver was very brave, punching Kilmen in the jaw, causing him to fall backward, resulting in two wild shots, one hitting General George and the other hitting the adjutant in the head. At this time, Kilmen stood up again, still holding his gun, but was simultaneously stabbed in the head by two mounted police officers, falling to the ground instantly. As the gunfire erupted, police also fired rifles, resulting in twenty people being injured, one of whom was Admiral Bedreau and three women. The crowd was furious and rushed forward, causing the guards to stop firing. The injured cried out in agony, and the crowd was shocked and terrified, running in all directions. The assassin was trampled. Soon the police were able to restore order, and the King's car slowly drove to the police station. Barthou's injuries were not discovered until the King was carried out of the car, and he was immediately taken to the hospital. The King died at 4:15 PM. At 5:00 PM, the doctors treating Barthou said that he was not in danger, but at 5:45 PM, Barthou also died. Although doctors performed a blood transfusion, it was ineffective. The adjutant died immediately, George lingered until 6:00 PM, and Count Jevtic died at 6:30 PM. At 8:30 PM, one of the injured guards also died. The provincial government here lowered the flag to half-mast at 5:00 PM, but at that time it was still unknown whether the deceased was the King or Barthou. (National News Agency, 9th)

Assassin's Background Investigated 43

Orim Party Instigated

Headquarters in Bulgaria

Marseille – Police have investigated the assassin of the King of Yugoslavia and Barthou, Kariman, who stayed two nights at a hotel in Aix-en-Provence (near Marseille) on Sunday and Monday. The hotel owner, after being shown a photo of the assassin, confirmed that the person who stayed there was indeed Kariman. The pattern tattooed on the assassin's arm (i.e., the letters VMRO, a skull, and the Bulgarian words "Freedom or Death") has been identified by police as the secret code of the "Orim" Party. The "Orim" Party is a secret organization whose purpose is to unite the lands inhabited by the Macedonian people. Its headquarters are located in Bulgaria, and all the disturbances in Yugoslavia are instigated by this group. The leader of the group, Michailov, has left Bulgaria for Turkey. Since the visit of the late King Alexander of Yugoslavia to Bulgaria at the end of last month to conclude a treaty between Bulgaria and Yugoslavia, Bulgarian Prime Minister Georgeff has ordered the dissolution of the "Orim" Party and told reporters that he was not afraid of any incidents after the dissolution. (Havas, 11th)

French Detective Squad Fully Mobilized (Paris) The National Detective Squad is now working hard to investigate the background of the assassin Kariman. Interior Minister Fondeur has ordered the police authorities to conduct a thorough study of the passport carried by Kariman to see if it is forged. In addition, the Ministry of Interior stated in the clearest terms that there was only one assassin and that the French police had not neglected any necessary protective measures. Before the King arrived in France, the police had been monitoring Yugoslavs who opposed the monarchy or belonged to the Croatian autonomy movement. The French police had also obtained a list of Yugoslav agitators from the Yugoslav Embassy in France, and those on the list who were in France were either monitored or deported. Many Yugoslavs with a record of bad behavior were arrested yesterday, and the contacts of other foreigners were also monitored. The precautions were very strict. (Havas, 10th)

Assassin's Passport Forged Belgrade It was said that there were demonstrations in Saragosa and Chaegribai today against the assassin of the King and the French foreign minister, Karmen, and that public calls for Italy's name were dispersed by the police, and it has now been proven that the assassin's passport was forged, and was never presented to the Czech consul in Chaegribai, and that an unemployed youth, Vavorina, was arrested in the Czech capital yesterday for having a passport with the same number as the assassin's passport, and it is said that he lost the passport, and the public initially thought he might have sold it to the forgery agency, but the police later stated that Vavurina's passport was in the possession of the government, and it was proved that Vavurina was innocent, and Karmen's passport was indeed forged (Reuters, 11th).

Tattoo of a Skull on His Arm The "Political Newspaper" correspondent in Marseille, the capital of Yugoslavia, reported that he witnessed the assassin's left arm tattooed with the letters VMRO, a skull, and the words "Freedom and Death" in Bulgarian. Since the assassin's passport was forged, the unimaginable pattern tattooed on his arm was probably deliberately designed to mislead and prevent investigation. According to general opinion here, the assassin was not a member of the Macedonian Revolutionary Party of Bulgaria, but a member of the terrorist "Ustasas" party of Yugoslavia. (Havas, 10th)

Yugoslav Capital The assassin of King Alexander, Carlman, has not yet been identified, and three people with the surname Carlman have been arrested, but it has been proven that they are indeed good people, and they have been released. A Spaniard named Carlman in the Zagreb area set off for Marseilles on October 6, and on October 9 he received a telegram in Marseilles, King Alexander

was undoubtedly using a code, and this person has not yet been found, and there are no traces of him in Marseilles or the Bulgarian capital. The assassin Carlman's false passport, which was obtained on May 30 of this year, was rumored yesterday to have been issued by the Czech consul in the city of Zagreb, but it has now been determined that this is not true, as the consul was not in the city of Zagreb at that time. In short, the assassin's passport is a Czech passport, his name is similar to that of a Hungarian, and his place of birth is Croatian, so the investigation is extremely complex. The assassin's left arm is tattooed with (the letters VMRO and a human skull). The newness of the tattoos is now being investigated, and if they are new tattoos, they must be to confuse people and make investigation difficult. (Havas, 11th)

Important Discoveries in the Hotel (Paris) The police investigation into the Marseille assassination has made several important discoveries. It is learned that the assassin and another Yugoslavian arrived in Paris on September 30 and stayed in a small hotel on Massalen Street. One signed the name Rudolf Szek, born in 1899 in Trieste, and the other signed the name Fulavoslav Pennasch, born in 1903 in Tsaraszek, which is undoubtedly the alias of the chief assassin, Kelman. Szek and Pennasch shared a room and met daily with another Yugoslavian named Maris, a well-known troublemaker who had committed several crimes. The three then went to Aix-en-Provence in southern France and stayed at the Modern Hotel. The hotel owner confirmed that the Marseille assassin was one of them. One of the three left the hotel on Monday morning, while the other two read various newspapers in the hotel. After breakfast, the two went out and returned to the hotel in the evening to pay their bills and collect their luggage, saying that they were in a hurry to leave due to some commercial relations. The police are now fully investigating the other two people who were with the assassin. Kelman was undoubtedly a revolutionary and the mastermind of the assassination. The group had sufficient funds, as the assassin used an automatic submachine gun worth 2,000 francs. The other pistol found on the assassin was also a state-of-the-art weapon of considerable value. The police have now searched the nests of Yugoslavian revolutionary groups in Paris, and French Foreign Minister Barthou

has arrested four people, including Radic, the son of the Croatian national leader who was shot and killed in the Yugoslavian parliament three years ago. There is no evidence to date that the four are related to the Marseille assassination. The police seized many documents, which are now under investigation. (National Telegram, 11th)

Accomplices Apprehended on the French-Swiss Border (Paris) Two suspects, Pinishu and Novac, were apprehended today at a certain hotel in Solen for conspiring with the assassin of the Southern King, Carlman. It is said that one of them confessed that if the assassination in Marseille had failed, they would have attempted it in Paris. The two were apparently planning to board a ship to Geneva and enter Switzerland (Reuters, 11th).

King's Coffin Transported Back 44

French Warships Escort Along the Way

Marseille - The coffin of King Alexander of the Southern Kingdom was carried aboard the cruiser "Dubrovnik" today for transport back to his country. First, French General Souchet and seven officers paid their final respects to the remains and played the national anthems of the Southern Kingdom and France. The procession then started from the Provincial Government Office in a somber atmosphere and passed through various thoroughfares to reach the wharf. A armored car full of wreaths led the way, followed by the coffin. President Lebrun, Queen Marie, the royal family of the Southern Kingdom, and the two ministers of the unrestrained cabinet, Herriot and Taitio, walked along carrying the shroud. Many people walked silently, following the procession. After the coffin arrived at the wharf, several Yugoslav officers carried the coffin onto the warship. Everyone present was silent for one minute. At 4:30 PM, the "Dubrovnik" set sail for the Southern Kingdom, escorted by two French cruisers and two destroyers. The Italian naval attaché in France recently inquired with the Navy Department about the time the "Dubrovnik" would pass through the Strait of Messina in Italy, saying that the Italian Navy would send warships to pay respects to the remains of the Southern King at that time. The French government has decided to close all schools in the country for one day this Saturday to commemorate the mourning of the two countries. (Havas, 10th)

Barthou's Remains Arrive in Paris 45

Placed in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for People to Pay Their Respects

State Funeral Set for Saturday

(Paris) The remains of the late Foreign Minister Barthou have been placed in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and will be available for public viewing from this afternoon until Saturday morning. To date, the remains have been guarded by his family and members of the Ministry. (Havas, 11th)

(Paris) At 6:00 PM, the coffin of the late Foreign Minister Barthou was transported from the Provincial Government Office in Marseille. President Lebrun and the two unrestrained cabinet ministers, Herriot and Taitio, were all present. The coffin, draped with the national flag, was transported directly to the station, accompanied to the capital by Herriot and Taitio. Many spectators lined the streets along the procession route, and the military played music to pay their respects. After the coffin arrived here, it was placed in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The state funeral will be held at 1:30 PM on Saturday. Only Premier Dumaige will deliver a speech at that time. Barthou's funeral will be kept simple according to his will, but the government intends to bury the remains in the Shrine of Loyalty. (Havas, 10th)

Purpose of the King's Visit to France 46

Marseille - This was the King's first official visit since the war, and the French side had made great efforts to arrange a particularly warm welcome. The purpose of his visit to France was to discuss important political events, to strengthen the friendship between France and the South, and to ease the tense relations between Italy and the South, which was a key point of this visit. To avoid passing through Austrian and Italian territory, the King embarked on a warship, and the French fleet and naval aircraft in the Mediterranean Sea all greeted him in Marseille, and the French naval chief personally greeted him at the pier. It was agreed that they would take a special train to Paris, while the Queen, unaccustomed to the rough seas, would travel by land and meet him in Paris. Unexpectedly, shortly after arriving in Marseille, this tragedy occurred. Crown Prince Peter, who is only eleven years old, is currently studying at Cobham School in Surrey, England. He will not be informed of this bad news for the time being, but will be notified after receiving official instructions.

The London diplomatic community was deeply shocked by this bad news, as the King was a key figure in maintaining peace in the Balkans. The fact that relations in various aspects of the Balkans are better today than before is due to the King's unremitting efforts. (Reuters, 10th)

An Officer's Eyewitness Account 47

According to the driver of the King's car, as the car approached the stock exchange, a strong man suddenly rushed out of the crowd, climbed onto the fender of the car, and fired four or five shots at the King and Barthou. He immediately grabbed his neck, and Colonel Pilot, who was riding alongside the car, also struck the man with his saber. Colonel Pilot described the situation to the Reuters reporter as follows:

"As the car carrying the King and Barthou approached the stock exchange, I saw a man rush out of the crowd, cross the police on the side of the street, and gallop to my horse. He jumped onto the fender of the car. I quickly spurred my horse to chase him, but it was too late. The man reached his arm through the window and fired an automatic pistol at the King. I knocked him down with my saber. The assassin rolled around on the ground, still firing his gun. The driver of the car also fired back with his pistol (Reuters, 10th).

Peter II Announced as Successor 48

Three Regents Appointed in Accordance with the Late King's Will

Future Policy Said to Be Shifting Towards Pro-British Stance

Belgrade – Just hours after receiving the official report from Paris late last night that King Alexander had been assassinated in Marseille, Crown Prince Peter, now eleven years old, was announced to have inherited the throne of Yugoslavia, a fact which came as a surprise, as it had been declared by Paris last night that the Crown Prince's succession would not be announced until several days later. The declaration of accession was based on Article 36 of the Constitution, and the new monarch was designated Peter II, and a regency was immediately established to handle state affairs until the new monarch came of age. The candidates were Prince Paul, the King's uncle, former Minister of Education Stegko Fovke, and Governor Polovich of Seff Province. Before dawn this morning, members of the cabinet and naval and military officers solemnly swore allegiance to King Peter II by torchlight. The cabinet then held a simple meeting and announced a six-month period of national mourning. News from London said that King Peter arrived in Gotham at 8:40 this morning and immediately changed cars to move forward, his whereabouts kept strictly secret (National Telegram, 10th).

Belgrade - King Alexander of Yugoslavia foresaw that the monarchs of Serbia rarely ended well, so he stated in his will that if he died and his son was still in school, the Crown Prince must return home to attend the funeral and then return to England to continue his studies. However, it is doubtful whether Peter, who is now supposed to succeed his father, will be able to return to England, as according to the Constitution, the King of Yugoslavia must reside in the country permanently. The Regency will today strive to form a strong government of national unity and gain the support of the people. There are no prominent politicians among the Regency, and they are welcomed as they have no partisan conspiracies (Reuters, 11th).

Belgrade - The Senate and House of Representatives held a joint meeting today to swear allegiance to the new king. The policy of the new regency will be friendly towards Britain, as the leader of the regency is approximately Prince Stanley Kavic, the former Minister of Education, who studied at Oxford University and has long advocated the British-style civil rule (Reuters, 10th).

New Monarch Studying in England, Returns Home Upon Hearing News, Now Safely Arrived in Paris 49

(Paris) The new monarch of the South has now arrived in Paris (Havas Telegram)

Belgrade - This morning, the newspapers published a formal announcement that Crown Prince Peter had succeeded to the throne of Yugoslavia. The new King, who was studying at Cobham School in Surrey, England, is hurrying back to the capital. The army and navy have sworn allegiance to the new monarch. The late King Alexander had ordered in his will that the former Minister of Education, Prince Stanley Kavic, and the Governor of Chai Koli White Province, Bantrovic, should organize the Regency.

This morning at 6:00 AM, the new King was urged by his Chief of Staff to quickly dress and see the headmaster. When he arrived at the headmaster's office, he was told the bad news. He hurriedly ate breakfast and, accompanied by his teacher and a detective, took a car to London, his face pale and his expression frightened, wearing a dark flannel suit and a school cap. At 9:00 AM, he arrived at the Yugoslav Embassy, where he saw the flagpole flying at half-mast, and was visibly abashed. Last night, due to the lack of official news and instructions, the news of his father's death was not immediately told to him (Reuters, 10th).

(London) When the headmaster told King Peter of Yugoslavia this morning that his father had died and that he had been crowned as the new King, his first words were, "I want to see my mother." The new King, who is only eleven years old, seemed very surprised to suddenly shoulder the heavy responsibility of a monarch. The new King, under strict police protection, traveled by car at a speed of 70 miles per hour, arriving at the Southern Embassy in London early this morning. He then met with several ambassadors and ministers from various countries in the embassy. British Foreign Secretary Simon also went to pay his respects and condolences. At noon, he went to Rich with his grandmother, Queen Mary, for lunch. At 2:00 PM, they went to Paris together. When boarding the car, the new King wanted to help his grandmother in first, but the Queen, because her grandson was now a monarch, let him board first. In the car, the new King took off his hat and stuffed it in the corner of the car. The Queen put her arm around him, as if to comfort him. At that time, the new monarch of Yugoslavia

did not know that his father had been assassinated, but thought that he had died in an accident. The train that the new King and Queen Mary were riding in was the ordinary Golden Arrow, but there was also a special car filled with police officers, escorting them to Dover, and there were military police patrolling the route. Detectives accompanied the new King on board, escorting him to Calais, France, and entrusting the responsibility of protection to the French police. France also sent several police officers to Dover to accompany the new King's ship across the English Channel (Reuters, 10th).

Brief History of the Yugoslav King 59

Ruler of Three Ethnic Groups: King Alexander of Yugoslavia was the second son of King Peter I of Serbia. After the establishment of the unified state of the three ethnic groups of Serbs, Croats, and Slovenes, he was crowned as the new monarch. His mother was the daughter of King Nicholas of Montenegro. King Alexander married the second daughter of King Ferdinand of Romania in June 1922 and had three sons. The King's task of ruling a new country composed of three ethnic groups was not easy. In addition, few of the ministers left by his father were friends and many were enemies, which made it even more difficult. According to the royal family's history, it was founded by his great-grandfather George. In 1804, George raised the banner of rebellion in Serbia and succeeded in resisting Turkey. From 1804 to 1813, he became the leader of the Serbian people. In 1903, his grandson Peter became king, and in 1921, he died, and his son, Crown Prince Alexander, succeeded him. Alexander had been regent since 1914, but he was not crowned until 1933.

Military Career: Alexander studied in Geneva and then at the Peter the Great Military Academy in St. Petersburg. After returning to his country, he applied what he had learned and served the country. From 1914 to 1918, he was almost always on the battlefield. During the first and second Balkan Wars, he repeatedly made military achievements as an ordinary soldier. During the European War, he always served as the commander-in-chief of the Serbian army. In 1915, the Serbian army suffered a disastrous defeat and retreated through Albania. Alexander refused to abandon his soldiers and save himself, willing to share their hardships, which revived morale. The King was brave and good at fighting, strong and enduring, inheriting the traits of his father and being resourceful and strategic, with much of the style of his maternal grandfather, King Nicholas of Montenegro, who was known as the "old fox" of the Balkans.

Exercising Absolute Power: King Alexander gradually eliminated his political enemies and implemented strict centralism, which made him unpopular. Because politicians and leaders of various factions were constantly fighting for power, he resolutely abolished the constitution on January 6, 1929, and implemented military rule, with his close friend General Živković serving as dictator. The government was only responsible to the King, with the aim of eliminating ethnic and historical differences among the people.

On November 7, 1929, he ordered the renaming of the country to Yugoslavia, which means "South Slavia." On October 3, 1931, the King promulgated a new constitution, nominally democratic, but in reality, the power was still in his hands.

Unity of Three Countries: In recent years, the King has made every effort to cooperate with Romania and Czechoslovakia in order to consolidate Yugoslavia's position in the Balkans. These three countries are known as the Little Entente. The meeting in Silezia in September 1933 was an important action to achieve this goal.

Brave and Skilled in Battle: The King's anecdotes are well-known among the people. In June 1915, when retreating through Albania, the monarch and government officials all boarded the first ship to flee to France. The King alone refused to leave, despite the danger of dying from artillery fire or being captured by the enemy, and calmly directed the troops to retreat to a safe place, which greatly enhanced his reputation. In early 1915, when Belgrade was abandoned, the government issued a strict order that no one was allowed to return to the capital, because the Allied forces were bombarding the main roads, and those who entered could not protect themselves. At that time, a car carrying two officers was stopped by the guards and ordered to retreat. One of the officers was King Alexander, who did not comply and still ventured to Belgrade, completed his important task, and returned to the Nish headquarters. Although the King was brave, he was also superstitious, like many old soldiers. He never dealt with political affairs on Tuesdays or Fridays. Whenever making major national decisions, he would go to the church built by King Peter in Topola at night and pray all night before his father's tomb.

Discord Among Brothers: The King's treatment of his brother George was widely criticized. During the European War, George made outstanding military achievements and was highly respected, but the King used party leaders as tools to implicate George in crimes. In 1924, he took the opportunity to place George in a private mental asylum near Nish, under heavy guard. It is said that George was harshly treated in the asylum.

Brief Biography of Barthou 60

Repeatedly Achieved Success in Diplomatic Negotiations

Can Be Compared with Briand

(Paris) The late Foreign Minister Barthou (surname), Louis (given name), was born in 1862. He studied in Pau as a child, and his grades were always the best in his class. At that time, Barthou was already fascinated by politics. He later graduated from the Faculty of Law at the University of Bordeaux and practiced law there. He then went to Paris for further studies, finally obtaining a doctorate in 1886. His two dissertations were widely praised. In 1888, Barthou served as a member of the Pau Municipal Council. The following year, he was elected as a member of the Chamber of Deputies. Later, he was transferred to the Senate for each joint election. In 1894, Barthou was only 32 years old when he became Minister of Public Works. He later served as Minister of the Interior and Minister of Justice, and in 1913, he formed a cabinet and served as Prime Minister. During the European War, his son was killed in battle. Barthou was deeply saddened and did not ask about political affairs. Later, at the urging of the late Prime Minister Painlevé, he joined the War Committee of the Cabinet as a Minister without Portfolio. After the signing of the Treaty of Versailles, the Chamber of Deputies passed the treaty based on Barthou's report. Since then, Barthou has held important positions in the cabinet and played an important role in domestic politics. For example, the law restoring the three-year term of military service, which was passed by the National Assembly when the European War was about to break out, was largely due to Barthou's efforts. Barthou was not only a politician but also a great orator, and he wrote many books on law and history. In 1918, he was elected to the Académie des Inscriptions et Belles-Lettres. (9th Havas News Agency)

(Paris) Foreign Minister Barthou was tragically assassinated in Marseille yesterday. Barthou was a leader in the French political world. He was first a member of the Chamber of Deputies in 1889, and then served as a cabinet member and other important positions before becoming Prime Minister. In 1922, he was re-elected as a senator. Barthou's most successful period was in the first year after the war. He represented France in negotiating difficult war debt issues, so Barthou was one of the most familiar with war debt issues. Barthou was born in Oloron-Sainte-Marie, near the Spanish border. He earned a doctorate in law and practiced law in Paris. He wrote about ten books in his lifetime, none of which were particularly good, but he was promoted to the French Academy for this and enjoyed immortal fame. Barthou had a rich collection of books. In 1894, Barthou was Minister of Public Works, and two years later, he was Minister of the Interior. He then served as Minister of Justice twice. In 1913, he overthrew Briand and became Prime Minister. He was later overthrown by Doumergue. Barthou belonged to the left wing. After serving as Foreign Minister in the current cabinet, he became a political leader in all of Europe. (10th National Telegram)

October 19th Reuter's Special Commodity Market Report 72

Gold and Silver: London Gold Price: Today (October 11th), the price of gold rose again to 143 shillings and 3 pence, 9 pence higher than yesterday's price.

Spot prices rose by 1.125 pence to 24.5 pence, and futures rose by 1.1875 pence to 24.625 pence. Chinese sellers emerged as prices rose, and the closing trend was uncertain.

Bombay Silver: Today, the silver market was firm and prices rose sharply, ranging from 1 rupee 13 annas to 1 rupee 14 annas. The spot closing price was 65 rupees 6 annas, the November contract was 65 rupees 7 annas, and the December contract was 65 rupees 11 annas.

At 11:00 AM, it continued to fall by another half point to $4.89. By noon, it rebounded by $0.000625. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, it fell by $0.00125 to $4.889375. The price remained unchanged at 2:00 PM.

Recent prices are still 1 to 5 points higher than the opening.
