Chiang and Zhang Go North Together to Luoyang 73

Hankou Correspondence: Chairman Chiang completed his public affairs in Hankou and was originally scheduled to go to Zhengzhou with Zhang Xueliang on the evening of the 8th, then transfer to Luoyang to attend the opening ceremony of the second phase of the Luoyang Military Branch School on Double Ten Day. Later, it was changed to the morning of the 9th. On the evening of the 8th, Chiang telegraphed from the executive headquarters in Jiangxi, summoning Luo Zhuoying, commander of the 18th Army, to Hankou to inquire about the situation of bandit suppression in Jiangxi Province. On the morning of the 9th, at 8:00 AM, Luo arrived by plane. After Chairman Chiang met him, he took a car and went north. Earlier, the Pinghan Railway Bureau had prepared a special train, parked at the Dazhimen Railway Station with the fire lit, and there was an armored car leading the way. At around 8:00 AM, Zhang Xueliang led his entourage, including advisor Duan Na, Chief of Staff Tan Hai, and Secretary-General of Chiang's Headquarters Yang Yongtai, secretaries Mao Qingxiang, Luo Junqiang, Chen Fang, director Yan Daogang, and Chief of Staff Xuan Tiewu, to board the train first. He Chengjun, Zhang Qun, Xu Yuanquan, Wu Xingya, Chen Guangzu, Ye Peng, Guo Rudong, Ding Bingquan, Huang Gongzhu, Wang Shaoyu, Zeng Qingxi, Tao Yaojie, Yang Xingqin, Wu Shaoshu, Li Jihong, Zhou Zechun, Chen Xizeng, Cai Mengjian and other important party, government, and military figures were all at the station to see them off. Military security was extremely tight. At 9:30 AM, Chairman Chiang boarded the train and immediately headed north. Zhang Xueliang told reporters before leaving that Chairman Chiang also served as the principal of the Luoyang Military Officer Branch School, and he served as a member. The opening ceremony of the second phase, after preparations by Education Director Ni Shaozhou, was scheduled to be held on Double Ten Day. He followed Chairman Chiang to participate and would not stay in Luoyang for long before returning to Hankou. He Yingqin, Chairman of the Peiping Military Branch, took a train south from Peiping on the 7th, originally planning to come to Hankou to visit Chairman Chiang and report on the military situation in North China. Upon learning that Chairman Chiang was about to go north, he changed his plans to visit him in Zhengzhou. Therefore, after arriving in Zhengzhou last night, He did not come south. Liu Zhi, director of the Henan Pacification Headquarters, also arrived in Bian yesterday to meet him and will go to Luoyang together. (October 9th)

Li Zongren Will Return to Guangxi 74

Guangxi Army Pursues and Suppresses Xiao's Bandits in Guizhou

Wang and You Cooperate Again in Guizhou Province

Guangzhou Correspondence: Li Zongren, commander-in-chief of the Fourth Group Army of Guangxi Province, went to Hong Kong on the 27th of last month to visit Hu Hanmin and discuss the overall situation. On the 3rd of this month, he returned to Guangzhou with his adjutant Qiu Chang. After breakfast at his private residence, he went to Chen Jitang's private residence in Meihua Village for a confidential talk for an hour. In the afternoon at 1:00 PM, Li and Chen went to the Southwest Political Affairs Council one after another to have a lengthy discussion with Xiao Focheng, Zou Lu, Deng Zhiru, and others until about 3:00 PM. It is said that Li is scheduled to return to Guangxi during the day and will meet with Bai Chongxi in Nanning. Bai had set off to the Liuzhou and Guilin areas to inspect defense affairs because the Guangxi army entered Guizhou to pursue and suppress Xiao's bandits. According to a recent telegram from Liao Lei, commander of the Guangxi army, Xiao's bandits were defeated in Menghai by the Li and Zhou divisions and attempted to flee northeast across Wang Bridge, but were intercepted by Wang Tuanming's battalion. Their situation was dire, and they fled back to Bagua River. Two regiments of the Guangxi army pursued and suppressed them toward Bagua River on the 26th of last month. The bandits were terrified and, after a brief encounter, fled to Daguan. The 2,000 to 3,000 people left in Banxi first fled to Daguan and were intercepted head-on by the Qin Division and the Independent Regiment and Cheng Brigade, killing three to four hundred bandits. The bandits in Bagua River were pursued by the Wang and Zhang regiments and fled in two routes from Banxi to Liangshang, with a tendency to flee north. In addition to sending the Qin Division to pursue and suppress them, the Guangxi army also moved the Li and Zhou divisions westward. Wang Jialie of the Guizhou army led his troops to Zhenyuan to block the river. From Bagua River to Pingliu, a two-day journey, many wounded bandits were abandoned along the way, and luggage and other items were everywhere. If they were severely attacked once or twice more, Xiao's entire bandit force could be disintegrated. According to the telegram, Bai said that Xiao's remaining forces had fled north. Once the inspection of military affairs in Liuzhou and Guilin was completed, he would return to Nanning to wait for Li Zongren. Bai has been paying close attention to Guizhou affairs recently. In addition to sending troops to assist Wang Jialie in attacking Xiao's bandits from both sides, he also advocated that the internal unity and solidarity of Guizhou Province should be unified as soon as possible to jointly defend against the Red bandits. Therefore, Wang has recently sent personnel to contact You Guocai. You also telegraphed Wang on the 26th of last month, expressing his sincerity in cooperation. Wang then personally went to Zhenyuan to command the bandit suppression and appointed You as the director of the Civil Affairs Department, acting as chairman of the provincial government. You has agreed to go to the province alone to discuss major plans. Yesterday, he also telegraphed Bai Chongxi, expressing his gratitude for his assistance in suppressing Xiao's bandits. Bai replied to You's telegram, saying, "Commander You of Xingyi, Yong Nong brother, Jian Dong, and Brother Deyi forwarded your telegram. I have read it carefully. The Red bandits are wreaking havoc in Guizhou, and the disaster is deepening. My brother loves the country and his hometown and can see the big picture. He goes to the province alone, openly and honestly, and befriends Lian Po and Lin Xiangru. This is a good story for thousands of years. Your magnanimous demeanor is admirable. In the future, we will cooperate in planning and seek major plans together. This is the fortune of Guizhou Province and the blessing of the Southwest. Bai Chongxi bows." (October 5th)

Xu Yongchang Talks About Controlled Economy in Shanxi Province 75

| To Save the Rural Areas, We Must Use Domestic Goods |

Peiping Correspondence: Xu Yongchang, chairman of Shanxi Province, came to Peiping a few days ago to attend the fifth general meeting of the Political Consolidation Committee. Today (October 9th), according to Xu, "I plan to suppress bandits because I still have private affairs to settle." (October 9th) He will stay in Peiping for more than ten days before returning to Taiyuan. Shanxi Province has implemented a controlled economy in recent years. The so-called control is actually just statistical work and a thorough investigation of the province's industries. Because various places are currently advocating saving the rural areas and revitalizing industry and commerce, we must know that to save the rural areas, we must first cultivate the people's strength. However, the first thing to do to cultivate the people's strength is to encourage the use of domestic goods. Therefore, the main purpose is to provide local products for local people to use. Since the Shanxi-Suiyuan Army implemented the disbandment, it can save 190,000 yuan per month. The head of the cabinet is still living in Hebian Village, serving the old man and recuperating from illness. Sun Dianying is still living in Jinci and is in good condition. Teams have been sent to Shenmu and Fugu to assist in suppressing bandits.

Northwest Inspection Notes by our special correspondent Geng Ya

A General Description of the Life of the Tibetan People in Qinghai (Part 2) 76

The language of the Tibetan people is entirely Tibetan. Although the tones vary due to the mountains and rivers in different regions, they are generally all from the same lineage of Tibetan. Among them, the Lhasa language is more popular and commonly used. Because the lamas in each temple all use the Tibetan script (i.e., Tibetan script), and there are no schools for education, those in the countryside who are literate rely on entering temples to recite scriptures. Therefore, all the text is purely Tibetan. Provincial and county announcements and official documents must also be in both Chinese and Tibetan. It is said that the British have established churches and hospitals all over Tibet, with attached schools, widely collecting children of the Tibetan people, imparting considerable science, and establishing a Tibetan military school in India, with a grand scale and complete teaching. All lecture notes are translated from English into Tibetan, and those who are proficient in Tibetan are used as professors. The depth and toxicity of their intentions is truly chilling.

The Tibetan people's hobbies, regardless of men, women, old or young, lamas and monks, all love tobacco and alcohol. Tobacco, such as snuff, dry tobacco, and water tobacco, is common everywhere. Cigarettes are also becoming popular, but no Tibetan people smoke opium. This is truly a good phenomenon. When relaxing and drinking, they like to listen to the Tibetan version of "Romance of the Three Kingdoms." Those who can read or recite this book are welcomed everywhere. In addition, because of the special social organization, young men and women often spend their rose-colored love lives freely in the green meadows. Therefore, the gentle and clear singing, like mournful and longing tunes, is like spring dawn in a flower-filled valley, with birds chirping in disorder. When travelers hear it, they have a sense of "I feel deeply about this." A few selected translated love songs are recorded as follows:

(1) The daughters of the nobles are like peach pits, but even the peaches on tall trees will ripen one day. (2) When the flowers have bloomed, the bees don't have to worry. When the love relationship is cut off, what is there to grieve about? (3) The love geese by the shallow water are willing to linger here for a long time. When the ice is firm and the lake is frozen, they have to fly resolutely to the horizon. (4) Take the beautiful flowers and offer them to the Buddha. The hummingbirds that depend on each other day and night also fly to other people's halls. (5) The supreme Buddha image, although I try hard to silently remember it, still doesn't enter my mind. But her graceful figure is always vaguely in front of my eyes. (6) If I use my sincere and earnest heart for you to learn Buddhism, why worry about not reaching the Western Paradise in this life? (Those who are deeply trapped in the net of love and cannot get out of it should read this and be awakened.) (7) My dear, will you be with me for a long time? She said, "Unless death separates us, we will never leave each other." (8) Obeying her psychology, I also sacrificed my Buddhist relationship. If I resolutely enter the mountains to practice, I will violate her wishes. (This contradictory phenomenon of not forgetting love when practicing Buddhism and not forgetting Buddhism when in love is not unique to Tibetan youth.) (9) When the pearl was in my house, I didn't know it was so precious. Now that it has been lost to others, its omnipotence is revealed. (10) If I can accompany my beloved in my heart for a long journey, then I will feel happy on the road even if my feet are not wearing shoes. (11) The full chest of melancholy is not enough to tell outsiders, fearing that the enemy will be happy and the lover will be sad. (12) You, my beloved who descended from the upper realm like a bean flower, I not only ask to live with you in this life, but also wish that we will spend the next life together.

There are many popular proverbs and idioms among the Tibetan people. A few examples are listed below. (1) I won't share, and you won't take. (That is, not giving even a small thing to others and not taking anything from others.) (2) When it rains, the road is not good. When you drink, people are not good. (3) A smart person wakes up with a word, and a good horse gallops away with a whip. (4) Many mouths have no doors, and there are no doors at crossroads. (That is, it is not easy to prevent mouths, and it is easy to enter a wrong path.) (5) As long as you eat venison, even if you are thin, don't worry too much. As long as you drink Songpan tea (tea produced in Songpan, which the Tibetan people like most), even if there is no butter tea, don't worry too much.

Because of the differences in customs, languages, and writing among the Tibetan people in Qinghai, and because they have not been effectively implemented with special politics and effective education, the officials who have been appointed to govern them have always disregarded the laws of the country. Moreover, the free laws they use to restrain violence and behavior are often unreasonable. For example, if there is hatred between two tribes, A suddenly sends someone to attack B and seize B's cattle, sheep, and property. A kidnaps the people and waits for ransom. But if B is prepared, kills the person sent by A, A will lead the people to besiege B and send the so-called "village elders" eight people to ask B to compensate for the loss of life. B knows that he is in the wrong and cannot resist, so he is willing to compensate for life. First, he gives the blocking soldiers property and gifts of one or two hundred gold, or several horses, and asks A to lift the siege, and then discusses the price of life. For example, the fine of ninety-nine eighty-one means that for each human life, Mao cattle, hybrid cattle, castrated sheep, yellow cattle, stallion horses, mares, camels, donkeys, and mules should each be compensated with nine heads. If B's power is strong and fights against A, and there are deaths and injuries on both sides, after mediation by C, another tribe, if A dies eight people and B dies ten people, then A should compensate B for two lives, and pay the financial gift as usual as above. In addition, if A and B have no previous grievances, but a person from A privately robs from B and is killed, the compensation must also be paid as usual. Moreover, the amount of compensation is not the responsibility of the murderer alone, but is shared by all the people. Therefore, the Tibetan people like to rob and kill, which is mostly caused by the environment. If B does not admit the murder or robbery, or if it is really a wrong, then another set of illusory and unfounded methods such as "branding oil pot," "grabbing an axe," "rolling a flour egg," and "gambling a death curse" will be used to decide to God. The two parties involved will lose money and hurt their bodies, and those who regard themselves as village elders (small heads of non-thousand-hundred-household princes and red card red insurance, that is, real old-brand robbers who bring disaster to others) will get the fisherman's benefit in vain. If the Tibetan people are confined to bad customs and evil examples and continue to harm their vitality, if a method is not found to eliminate them, it will not be a good plan for curbing the border and pacifying the people.

The Tibetan and Mongol peoples are the two major ethnic groups surrounding the Northwest in our country geographically. In history, they had a close relationship as early as thousands of years ago. Therefore, the lives of the two ethnic groups are very similar. The first nomadic life and the strong belief in Lamaism are the common characteristics of the Mongol and Tibetan peoples. They wear Buddha statues, provide for Buddhas at home, and recite scriptures before every meal, offering food to heaven and earth before eating. Even more so, after death, they give all the accumulated property to the temple, saying that they ask the Buddha to keep it for them, and they can still use it in the next life. When people and animals are sick, they are superstitious about the lamas' scriptures and spells, and do not seek medical treatment or medicine. If there is something happy, they say that it is a gift from God and must think of a way to repay it. If there is something they don't want, they say that it is a punishment from God and they must make a wish to exorcise it. Whether it is exorcising or repaying, it all goes back to the lamas making money. Therefore, the number of temples is increasing day by day, and the status of lamas is also increasing day by day. They sit and eat in peace and enjoyment, and the number of disciples is also increasing day by day. On the contrary, the population of secular people who are engaged in production is decreasing day by day. Moreover, Mongol and Tibetan youths can have wild combinations at will in the mountains and grasslands, and they break their bodies too early, so many do not reproduce, which is also one of the reasons for the decrease in population. In addition, they are superstitious about "good days," such as the first, thirteenth, fifteenth, and thirtieth days of each month, they do not kill cattle and sheep, or they pick good days and discard bad days, such as the nineteenth is a good day, the twentieth and twenty-first are not good, then they discard the twentieth and twenty-first and spend three consecutive days of the nineteenth, squeezing horse, cow, and sheep milk every morning and evening, making meals, herding livestock, drawing water, grinding noodles, and entertaining guests are all concentrated on the wives and daughters, who are extremely hard-working. Men, except for sewing clothes, mostly have no proper business. Moreover, the Mongol and Tibetan people like to inquire about news. When they see pedestrians on the road, whether they know them or not, they must ask them courteously. If they get something, they must spread it widely. Therefore, events that occur in the grassland are transmitted very quickly. These are all common customs of the Mongol and Tibetan peoples.

As for the national character of the Mongol and Tibetan peoples, there are differences. Especially in the Qinghai area, the people of the two ethnic groups who come into contact with each other initially cause conflicts in life due to the differences in their temperaments. The Tibetan people are strong and brave, while the Mongol people are weaker. The Tibetan people regard robbery and looting as capable, while the Mongol people regard being a robber as a disgrace. Although the men of both ethnic groups wear swords and knives, and are good at riding horses and shooting, if there is any dispute and they draw their swords at each other, most of the Mongol people will avoid it, and the Tibetan people will show off their strength. Or if the Mongol people are robbed by the Tibetan people, they often dare not pursue them, fearing that chasing and injuring people will cause them to lose their property and have to pay compensation for life. It is better to save trouble. Therefore, the twenty-nine banners of the original Mongol people in Qinghai used to spread along both banks of the Yellow River. Now, the Tibetan people's land is expanding day by day, and the Mongol people's land is shrinking day by day. As a result, the Mongol people in Henan have disappeared, and the Hebei are gradually unable to support it. Although the Mongol and Tibetan people have the strengths and weaknesses, they have the common habit of knowing the law but not knowing gratitude, and fearing power but not cherishing virtue. In the future, we should actively promote Mongol and Tibetan education, take advantage of the situation, and correct their prejudices, so that we can unite sincerely and not be deceived by foreigners.

Tea Trade Depression in Southern Fujian 77

Affected by Reduced Exports to Nanyang

Xiamen Correspondence: Fujian Province is known for its tea production, with the producing areas being Wuyi in northern Fujian and Anxi in southern Fujian. Xiamen is a distribution center for tea in southern Fujian, supplying consumption in this province and exports to other provinces and overseas. Five or six years ago, the tea trade was extremely prosperous, with over a hundred tea firms. In recent years, due to the impact of the downturn, Nanyang's commerce has been sluggish, suffering a major blow. This year, only Yaoyang, Qiyuan, Jintai, Huang Quanpu, Fangmao, Jinxiang, Yuxiang, Chongmao, Wanchun, Wanquan, Wanfa, Deyi, Nanyan, Yanquan, Sanyang, Fusheng, Xiechang, Quanmao, Jinchun, Kecheng, Chun, Longfang, Xiuzhi, Ji, Meifanghui Ji, Wenji, Longquan, Chafang, Ganpu, Qingji, Minzhang, and more than 70 other smaller tea firms are selling Wuyi and Anxi tea. According to a recent survey, more than 30,000 boxes of Xicha are sold annually, half of which are sold locally and half of which are exported to the British and Dutch colonies in Nanyang. The British territories have lighter taxes, so they account for more. In recent years, the Nanyang economy has been weak, and sales channels have become narrower, and tea prices have also fallen. Over the years, the number of exports to Nanyang has gradually decreased. Xiamen's tea industry mainly sells to Nanyang, so the current situation is not as good as before, and sales have decreased to two-thirds of what they used to be. Currently, there are more than 70 tea firms left, among which only a few larger ones can maintain their operations. Most of the others are losing money. The larger ones such as Yaoyang and Qiyuan sell about one hundred and forty to fifty yuan a day in retail and wholesale (excluding exports to foreign countries). Next, Jintai, Huang Quanpu, Fangmao, and Jinxiang sell fifty or sixty yuan a day, and Yuxiang, Chongmao, Wanchun, Wanquan, Wanfa, Deyi, Nanyan, and Yanquan sell twenty or thirty yuan a day. Others sell only ten or twenty yuan, or less. Very few can maintain their operations. Therefore, tea firms have been closing down year by year. At the end of last year, more than 20 firms closed down, and tea prices plummeted. Tieguanyin, which used to sell for three yuan a box, is now only selling for two yuan and three corners. Other Oolong and narcissus teas have also fallen in price. However, high-end teas such as Wuyi famous varieties have not risen or fallen much, but these are luxury items for a small number of people and do not help the tea industry. However, sales have also been declining recently, and the number of people who like high-end tea is gradually decreasing. (6th)

Songjiang

Maple Creek Yao Clan Robbed 78

In Maple Creek, in this county, the Yao clan of Zha Jia Creek in the sixteenth district, lived together as a family, their household relatively prosperous. But unexpectedly, on the night of the eighth, around eleven o'clock, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived, speaking with a mixed local and migrant accent. Each held handguns and bayonets, and they violently crashed into the main gate. The head of the household, Yao Ruishan, knowing it was unavoidable, went to open it. But the bandits, unable to wait, immediately fired a shot, the bullet shattering the gate and hitting Ruishan's right shoulder. He supported his wound and fled into the inner room. The bandits swarmed in. Yao Delong, startled awake in his bed, got up and went to the front hall to investigate. The bandits, without asking any questions, stabbed him fiercely in the head with a bayonet, causing one wound to his right eyebrow and another to his left arm. The Yao family's various houses, including those of Delong, Zigan, Shushan, Ruishan, Zhushan, and Tumu, were successively robbed, none spared. The bandits lingered for about an hour before fleeing with their loot. The gold and jewelry stolen from Yao Zigan's wife were the heaviest losses, while Tumu's were lighter. The head of the household reported the incident to the Second Branch of the Public Security Bureau, who dispatched police to investigate. Six bullet casings were found inside and outside the Yao family's main gate. The branch bureau has reported the situation to the Public Security Bureau, requesting them to order an arrest.

Xingye Bank Collapses Due to Liabilities 79

The Shanghai headquarters of the China Xingye Bank established branches in both Suzhou and Songjiang in the past. The Songjiang branch was located at the original site of the former Songjiang Bank. Not long after it opened, it was robbed. Manager Yin Shisheng resigned to pursue other business ventures. The headquarters sent Wang Ming to Songjiang to take charge. In recent years, business had been stable and gradually improving. But suddenly yesterday, news arrived from Shanghai that the headquarters manager, Qin Baoyuan, had absconded with funds and could not make ends meet. The China Qunyi Banking Syndicate and the China Xingye Bank jointly appointed lawyer Zhang Ding and accountant Xu Chao to notify creditors to register their claims within two weeks to facilitate liquidation. Debtors are also required to submit payments directly to the firm within the same period to obtain receipts, otherwise lawsuits will be pursued.

Suzhou

Attempted Robbery by Bandits Thwarted 80

Since January, Suzhou has experienced three consecutive robberies, none of which have been solved. It has now been learned that the Zhang family at No. 46 Royal Abandoned Base in the city was targeted for robbery by five or six bandits on the night of the ninth, around eight o'clock. Unexpectedly, the Detective Team learned of the plot and dispatched a large number of detectives to ambush the vicinity. Just as the bandits were about to enter the door, they were surrounded by detectives. The bandits Pan Hongxi, Wu Si, Qin Yuansan, Shen Asan, Li Youxian, and Lu Rukun, among others, six in total, were arrested. A wooden pistol was also seized. They were taken to the team headquarters. According to Pan Hongxi's confession, he admitted to the attempted robbery. He also confessed that on the fifth, he and Shen Asan, a blind man, had committed a robbery at Meicun Bridge outside Pingmen, and on August 17, they robbed pilgrims at Shihukou. They were handed over to the Public Security Bureau yesterday for interrogation.

Jiading

Hou Huang Bridge Constructed on the Xihu Road 81

The Xihu Road passes through this county, from southeast to northwest, its route quite long. There are dozens of bridges throughout the county, with the one spanning the Lianqi River outside the West Gate being the tallest. The County Chronicle Preparatory Committee, considering that the county's Ming Dynasty figures Hou Zhenyang, Hou Tongzeng, Hou Qizeng, and Huang Chunyao, Huang Jianyao and other martyrs raised armies to defend the city when the Qing troops descended, remaining unyielding through three massacres, and ultimately sacrificing their lives, believed that in this time of foreign aggression, these national heroes should be regarded as role models, widely promoted to inspire the people and encourage the customs. Therefore, the committee sent a letter through the County Education Bureau to request Education Director Zhou Fohai to name the bridge Hou Huang Bridge, so that those who pass by would know the lofty character and heroic integrity of Hou and Huang, and be moved by it. The Education Department has signed and forwarded the request to the Construction Department, which has agreed. Construction is currently underway.

Wuxi

Series of Robbery Cases Solved 82

Zheng Xianting, a resident of Zhengwan Village, Luoxia Bridge, in the Third District, has always been engaged in farming, owning more than thirty acres of good land. The day before yesterday, at twelve o'clock late at night, seven or eight bandits suddenly arrived, forced their way in through a side door, dragged Zheng's mother and daughter off the bed, and beat them, causing injuries to their waists and abdomens. They stole about seven or eight hundred yuan in gold, silver, and cash, and also stole a Mauser rifle. The rifle was later found in a nearby river. The next morning around three o'clock, Wang Huaiqing, a guard officer from the Third Branch of the South Gate police station, discovered two bandits, Wang A____ and Yang Ziqing, at Bode Harbor. They were taken to the station for interrogation and handed over to the Public Security Bureau yesterday, who transferred them to the local court for questioning. In addition, at Gao Fan's house in Beichang Village near Zhang Village in the northern countryside, several bandits broke in and robbed the house. They tied up Gao Fan and her son, Peigen. Unsatisfied, the bandits went to Gu Gao's house to rob, causing considerable losses. Later, Duan Qishan, the chief of the Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, captured three key suspects in the case, Ma Ronghai, Hua Asan, and Zhang Yichang, in the mulberry fields near No. 1 Bridge on the Xicheng Road. After being taken to the station, they were transferred to the General Bureau for interrogation. At the same time, Ma Zemin, a patrol officer from the Houqiao Directly Subordinate Second Outpost, arrested three bandits, Gao Zhiqing, Wang Yunshi, and Jiang Hongru, in Houqiao Town. During interrogation, they confessed to robbing the late Hua ____ Jingfan's house in Lao Xizhuang, No. 422, Beishang Township, in the Seventh District. They were handed over to the General Bureau yesterday for disposal.

Quack Doctor Causes Death by Mistreatment 83

Yu Aquan, a resident of Lihua Village, near the Irrigation Association, is 28 years old and a farmer. His wife, Zhao, is 22 years old and works as a female worker in a yarn factory. She is six months pregnant. Recently, Zhao suddenly felt unwell and went to Liu Zhensheng, the owner of the Wudetang Pharmacy in Zhoushan Harbor, for treatment. After examining her, Liu gave her a packet of medicine and instructed her to decoct and take it. Unexpectedly, after taking it, she developed a high fever and chills, and her abdomen was in excruciating pain. Her condition became very serious. She returned to Liu for treatment. Liu prescribed another prescription, instructing her to swallow the medicine. However, not only did it not help, but after taking it, the abdominal pain became even more severe. In less than two hours, the six-month-old fetus was expelled, and she was on the verge of death. Her husband, Yu Aquan, seeing this, immediately dragged Liu Zhensheng to the jurisdiction's Sixth Branch of the Public Security Bureau for investigation. He also reported to the local court, requesting an examination. Lian, the prosecutor, accompanied by Wang, the investigative clerk, went to examine her. The examination revealed that Zhao's condition was critical, the fetus was dead, and it was indeed caused by the prescribed medicine. After the examination, they returned to the court to report and await further instructions.

Earthquake on National Day Lasts One Minute 84

The day before (October 10th), around four o'clock in the morning, residents were still asleep. At that time, an earthquake suddenly occurred, moving from north to south, lasting for about one minute before stopping. Boxes and cabinets in the room were shaken and rattled. Urban residents mostly did not get up, so few knew about it.

Changshu

Qian Kidnapping Case: Seven Bandits Transferred to Changshu 85

Shoubao, the young son of Qian Lisan from Tangjia Bridge in the Fourth District of this county, was kidnapped by bandits. He was rescued from danger by the Suzhou Water Police District Department in Nanjin Bridge in the latter part of last month. The bandits Yang Genshou, Zhang Yousheng, Wu Jinhuo, Chang Gensheng, Zhao Fanshi, Cheng Shousheng, and Cheng Chenshi, men and women, totaling seven, were arrested. The hostage was first notified to be claimed by his family. The bandits were temporarily detained in the district department. Because the case occurred in Changshu, the Public Security Bureau believed that it should be tried in this county. They prepared an official document and sent the Detective Team, led by Li Fu and others, to Suzhou to escort them. They were escorted back to Changshu on the eighth and immediately handed over to the County Justice Department. Judge He interrogated them overnight, and the interrogation of the seven bandits lasted until around two o'clock this morning (the ninth). According to the bandits' confessions, there were still two ringleaders at large. There were a total of fourteen people involved in this case, and they had a long-standing feud with the Qian family, which is why they resorted to this vicious act.

Nantong

Kidnapping Bandit to be Sentenced to Death 86

Xu Mingyuan's family in Pingchao, Tongyi, was robbed by bandits, and his six-year-old grandson was kidnapped. Fourteen men and women involved in the case have been arrested in Tong and Shanghai. They were transferred to the court by the county government, and the prosecutor's office has completed its investigation. The prosecutor intends to sentence the ringleaders Xu Xinfa, Qiu Keqing, and Gu Chunsheng to death and has filed a public prosecution with the Criminal Court.

Cotton Control Association to Improve Nantong Homespun 87

The Cotton Control Committee believes that the sales of Nantong homespun are declining and its reputation is deteriorating. Without improvement, it is impossible to salvage the situation. Therefore, Li Shengbo, a standing committee member of the committee, accompanied by several specialized cotton weaving technicians, came to Tong to inspect manual weaving in the countryside. Li and others advocated starting with the improvement of iron looms. The technicians first returned to Shanghai to design and manufacture iron looms, which were transported to Tongyi to be imitated by weaving households. At the same time, Li raised funds to establish an electric dyeing factory in Tianshenggang. The site has been determined to be thirty acres of land west of the Dasheng Power Plant, and construction has begun.

Yangzhou

Earthquake Occurs in Yangzhou City 88

At 4:35 a.m. on National Day, a strong earthquake suddenly occurred in Yangzhou, lasting for about 35 seconds. The direction of origin and termination was from southwest to northeast. Roof tiles and window frames made rattling noises, and door knockers clanged. Walls shook and seemed about to collapse. People were awakened from their dreams, feeling as if they were lying in a boat being tossed by waves or sitting in a car traveling on an uneven road for about ten minutes.

Gaoyou

Gang Bandit of Da Li Village Defeated 89

The provincial government, concerned about the rampant gang bandits in the northeastern countryside of this county, ordered the fourth regiment commander of the Provincial Security Team to lead troops to suppress them. The first battalion commander ____ engaged the gang bandits in Suojia Village. The bandits were unable to withstand the attack and scattered. As a result, the bandit momentum was somewhat suppressed. Yesterday, several dozen gang bandits suddenly came, impersonating government troops and searching ships. At that time, the soldiers of the regiment, disguised as boatmen, used machine guns and box guns to fire at the gang bandits. The bandits were unable to resist and abandoned their weapons to flee. Five people were injured on the spot, and eighteen bandits were captured alive. Around four o'clock in the afternoon, after passing through Da Li Village, the five injured were killed. The eighteen captured alive were taken to the Linze Regiment Headquarters for interrogation. In addition, many kidnapped hostages in the Tanghe and Gaoqiao areas of the Fifth District have been released back to Haimen.

Attempted Robbery by Gang Bandits Foiled 90

Yesterday afternoon, more than ten bandits suddenly came to Miaoqiao Town in the Second District of Qidong, disguised as travelers, scattered on the streets, intending to wait for an opportunity to rob. However, Xing Zhenpeng and other merchants and residents of the town noticed them and gathered more than ten people, each carrying self-defense weapons, to search the area. Seeing the unfavorable situation, the bandits retreated and opened fire to resist arrest. Xing and others bravely pursued, capturing one bandit, Yu Chengchang, and seizing a pistol. The remaining bandits escaped. Yesterday, Yu and the pistol were handed over to the county government for interrogation.

Widespread Private Opium in Various Townships 91

The registration of opium addicts in this county has been extended to the 21st of this month. Opium paste shops in various districts have not been established. Taking advantage of this period, general opium dealers are actively operating, and some are being sheltered by evil forces. As a result, private opium is widespread in various townships, becoming more and more serious. The County Anti-Opium Committee dispatched personnel yesterday to conduct secret investigations.

Ningbo

Guard Executed by Firing Squad for Selling Red Pills 92

Zhao Zhenguo, a guard soldier from Taizhou serving in the Ningbo Defense Command, was found selling red pills (opium) by the Defense Commander. Zhao Zhenguo was detained and sent to Zhao Cisheng, the Administrative Inspector Commissioner of the Fifth Special District of Zhejiang and Military Judge of the Nanchang Headquarters, for trial. Commissioner Zhao, considering that the case involved a soldier selling red pills, telegraphed the Nanchang Headquarters and asked Chairman Chiang for instructions for the sake of caution. Yesterday, an order was received from Nanchang instructing that the criminal be executed on the spot as a warning to others. After receiving the order, Commissioner Zhao sent the original order and the criminal to the Defense Command for execution. After receiving the order, the Defense Command brought forward the criminal, verified his identity, and executed him by firing squad at Caoma Road on the north bank of the river at three o'clock yesterday afternoon.

Township Robbery Causes Injury in Jiaqing 93

Zhou Dingsheng and Zhou Decheng, neighboring residents of Shuangqiao in Jiaqing Township, eastern Yin County, recently invited relatives Cai Yao and others to their home to watch a play performed at the Zhou Family Ancestral Hall in the township. Around two o'clock last night, seventeen or eighteen bandits suddenly arrived, each carrying weapons. They broke into the homes of Decheng and Dingsheng by smashing the gates with stones and began robbing. Unexpectedly, one of the bandits, Li Asi, was recognized by Cai Yao. Cai Yao called out, "Brother Asi, please don't hurt anyone." Seeing that the secret was out, the bandit fired four shots in a row, hitting Cai Yao in a vital area, causing her to fall to the ground unconscious. Seeing that they had caused trouble, the bandits, along with the bandits from the neighboring house, fled in a panic. The two families suffered losses of more than three hundred yuan. Afterward, Cai Yao was sent to Yongbu Huamei Hospital for treatment. Due to the severity of her injuries, her life is feared to be in danger.

City News

Citywide Celebration of National Day Anniversary 94

Representatives from All Sectors Convene Commemoration Meeting

Military and Government Agencies Jointly Hold Celebration

Central News Agency reports, the day before yesterday was the 23rd anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China. All sectors of the city held a people's memorial meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce. The Municipal Government and the Garrison Headquarters also held a joint military-government commemorative meeting and award ceremony in the Municipal Government Auditorium in the city center. The Municipal Government and the Huinan area held review ceremonies. Boy Scouts from all over the city also held a flag-raising ceremony at the public stadium. The details of each event are described below:

Commemorative Meeting of All Sectors 95

The day before yesterday, all sectors held the 23rd anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China commemorative meeting at the City Chamber of Commerce in Tianhou Temple Bridge. Representatives from various agencies, groups, party headquarters at all levels, and schools attended the meeting. The presidium included Pan Gongzhan (Party), Zhang Yuanruo (Government), Yu Zuoting (Commerce), Wu Xiu (Education), Yu Zhenhui (Agriculture), and Shao Xubai (Industry). More than 500 representatives from all sectors attended the meeting.

A Glimpse of the Venue: The gate of the City Chamber of Commerce was decorated with the Party and National flags and red and green lanterns. A bamboo cloth banner was hung with the words "Shanghai City Representatives Commemorate the 23rd National Day Anniversary Meeting." On both sides of the venue, various colored slogans were posted. In front of the rostrum, a slogan was hung on the right, an order of events was hung on the left, and a banner with the words "Shanghai City Representatives Commemorate the 23rd National Day Anniversary Meeting," the Party and National flags, and a portrait of Sun Yat-sen were hung in the center. The venue arrangement was especially solemn.

Chairman's Report: After the ritual, the chairman, Pan Gongzhan, gave a report, saying in brief: In this time of national crisis, commemorating National Day, on the one hand, feels happy, on the other hand, feels very painful. In this situation, we feel that it is useless to not struggle upward and move forward, but only to shed tears. We recall the difficulties of the founding of the nation by the past martyrs, and we must summon up the utmost courage to fight desperately. Sun Yat-sen told us that the revolution has not yet succeeded, and comrades still need to work hard. The purpose of the national revolution is to seek freedom and equality. Now, who dares to say that China has obtained freedom and equality? The Xinhai Revolution certainly occupies an important page in the entire history of the national revolution. Today, we commemorate the fighting spirit of the martyrs and should summon our courage and exhaust our energy to continue to complete their unfinished cause. In other words, commemorating the past is for creating the future. The great achievements of the Xinhai Revolution are that it overthrew the autocratic system that had been passed down for thousands of years. Revolutionary volunteers under Sun Yat-sen's leadership exchanged blood and flesh for the establishment of the Republic of China. However, now the internal and external reactionary forces are intensifying their oppression of us, making the national crisis increasingly severe. May I ask if saving the nation is possible with partisan strife, each occupying one side? Now, we must abandon our private views and fight for the entire nation. First, we must be of one mind; second, we must cooperate. If we can be of one mind and cooperate, then the Chinese nation will not only save itself, but also become an invincible and powerful nation in the world. What should we work hard for with one mind and cooperation? First, productivity; second, defense force; third, organizational force. We must support a revolutionary leader to lead us to strengthen these three forces before the country can be strong and the nation can be revived. After the chairman's report, there were also speeches by Zhang Yuanruo, Wu Zhihao, and others. The speeches were lengthy and slightly ____. Slogans and Banners: Slogans: (1) October 10th is the anniversary of the revival of the Chinese nation. (2) Commemorating National Day requires promoting the New Life Movement. (3) Commemorating National Day requires suppressing the Red bandits. (4) Commemorating National Day requires striving for production and construction. (5) Prepare strength to recover lost territories. (6) Support revolutionary leader Chiang Kai-shek. (7) Long live the Kuomintang of China. (8) Long live the Republic of China. Banners: (1) Commemorating National Day, do not forget the difficulty of Sun Yat-sen and the martyrs in creating the Republic of China. (2) Commemorating National Day requires striving to resist Japan, wipe out humiliation, and seek revenge. (3) Commemorating National Day requires suppressing the Red bandits and stabilizing society. (4) Commemorating National Day requires actively producing and strengthening national power. (5) Sincerely unite to ensure peace and unification. (6) Support the government in implementing construction work. (7) Compatriots across the country, unite and prepare to recover lost territories. (8) October 10th is the glorious anniversary of the revival of the Chinese nation.

Joint Military and Political Commemoration 96

All departments and bureaus under the Shanghai Municipal Government, and the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, held a joint military and political National Day commemoration meeting in the Municipal Government Auditorium in the city center. Mayor Wu led the ceremony and delivered a report.

Attendees: Those who attended the meeting included Mayor and Commander Wu Tiecheng, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government Yu Hongjun, Director of the Security Bureau Yang Hu, Director of the Land Bureau Jin Liren, Director of the Health Bureau Li Ting'an, Director of the Public Utilities Bureau Xu Peihuang, Chief of Staff of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters Xu Jinyuan, Adjutant General Gan Hailan, as well as all staff members of the various bureaus and departments under the Municipal Government and the Garrison Headquarters, totaling more than a thousand people.

Mayor's Report: After the formalities, Mayor Wu delivered the following report: "Comrades, today is the National Day of the 23rd year of the Republic of China. All civil servants, military police, and community members of Shanghai are holding this National Day commemoration ceremony here. Looking back on the past, observing the present, and planning for the future, we have unlimited feelings in our hearts. The Republic of China has been established for 23 years. During these 23 years, despite the efforts, struggles, and sacrifices of all our party comrades and the people of the whole country, we have not yet been able to make China rich and strong, nor have we been able to make China stable. Since September 18th, we have encountered an unprecedented blow, forming the most serious national crisis in China's history. We are examining why the Chinese revolution has not yet succeeded and why we have encountered such a major blow in the process of the revolution. The reasons are no more than the following: First, when the Xinhai Revolution succeeded, most of our party comrades believed that the revolution had succeeded. At the same time, the party's organization was not sound, and comrades did not have a deep understanding or earnestly implement the Premier's revolutionary doctrine and revolutionary strategy. Therefore, there was a common saying among the revolutionary comrades at that time, 'The revolutionary army is with us, the revolutionary party is gone.' At that time, the revolution had not yet succeeded, but the spirit of the group had already declined and disintegrated, the unity was not strong, and the strength was not sufficient. There is no doubt that the revolution could not be completely successful. This is the first reason. Second, before the Xinhai Revolution, our doctrine was not widely publicized among the people, and they did not thoroughly understand the revolutionary doctrine, thinking that the revolutionary movement was just a racial revolution, a revolution against the Qing Dynasty and restoring the Ming Dynasty. Therefore, after the Xinhai Revolution overthrew the Qing Dynasty, the people of the whole country also believed that the revolution had succeeded. Under such circumstances, the revolutionary party could not but make a compromise. This compromise planted the seeds of disaster for more than 20 years.

Although we dare not say that this disaster can destroy China, it is enough to make China lag behind the world's surging torrent by 50 or 60 years. What is this disaster? It is the northern shift of the revolutionary government, the election of Yuan Shikai as the president, which led to the rule of warlords such as Yuan Shikai, Xu Shichang, Feng Guozhang, and Cao Kun, who used improper power to sell the country and only sought their own selfish interests. Because of this disaster, China has experienced small wars every half year and big wars every year for more than 20 years, with endless civil wars. Because of this disaster, the republican system has been shaken several times, so there was Zhang Xun's restoration and Yuan Shikai's稱 Emperor. These reasons have caused serious and unprecedented turmoil in China's politics and society, and China's national strength has declined day by day. Although the reasons for our current national crisis are very complicated and are caused by various national pathologies accumulated over nearly a century, if our party comrades could thoroughly implement the Premier's revolutionary doctrine and revolutionary strategy at the time of the Xinhai Revolution, if our revolutionary organization could be as united and strong as before the Xinhai Revolution, and if the revolutionary comrades could continue to work hard with the spirit of risking their lives with guns and bombs in more than a dozen revolutionary uprisings before the Xinhai Revolution, I believe that the Xinhai Revolution would not have been incomplete. If the Xinhai Revolution could be thorough, there would definitely not be Yuan Shikai. Without Yuan Shikai, there would be no arrogance of warlords, no restoration of Zhang Xun, and no civil wars for more than 20 years, which would have made the whole country unstable and the people unable to live. Nor would the national crisis have occurred so quickly, nor would the national crisis have been so serious today. If all party comrades could have the kind of strong unity and spirit of sacrifice before the Xinhai Revolution, and if the people of the whole country could also thoroughly understand the revolutionary doctrine and enthusiastically support the revolutionary movement, then even if we had this kind of national crisis, we would certainly be able to deal with it very calmly and confidently. The Shanghai War of January 28th, 1932, was not only heard by the citizens of Shanghai, but also witnessed by them. This war gave us a great lesson. At the time of the January 28th Shanghai War, if the country was unified, without the division between Ning and Yue, and without the scourge of the communists, our central government would certainly be able to command with ease, and be able to deal with the January 28th War with unity from top to bottom. Although our weapons were old and clumsy, our army would not have only resisted for more than 30 days, and the good impression that the Chinese nation gave to the world would certainly be even greater. Therefore, comrades, although the revolutionary party and the people of the whole country have made long-term efforts, struggles, and sacrifices for 23 years since the Republic of China, not only have they failed to make the revolution completely successful, not only have they failed to make all parts of the country stable, but they have also encountered an unprecedented national crisis. We cannot but blame those who undermine China's unity, we cannot but blame the disunity within the party, and we cannot but blame the fact that the people of the whole country have not thoroughly understood the revolutionary doctrine and have not contributed all their strength to the revolution. Therefore, on the occasion of the National Day of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, we should deeply recognize the lessons of this painful history. At the same time, I cannot but express my earnest expectations to the citizens. First, I hope that the citizens of Shanghai will not only carry out a widespread and powerful propaganda, but also take the lead in believing in a doctrine, the Three Principles of the People, so that the people of the whole country will believe in the Three Principles of the People, because the Three Principles of the People is the highest principle for us to be human beings and save the country. This is the first hope. Second, I hope to safeguard the unity of the country. If there are those who undermine the unity of the country, we will use all our strength to deal with them and stop them, so as to avoid the division of the country. The third hope is to support a revolutionary leader, because in the unstable situation of the country and the situation of not knowing what to do, we can only support a leader, and under the leadership of a leader, we can jointly carry out the revolutionary movement and jointly carry out the national salvation movement. Believing in a doctrine, supporting national unity, and supporting a leader are the most necessary conditions for saving the country and ensuring survival, and it is also the most effective way to save the country and ensure survival. We have had National Day every year since the 23rd year of the Republic of China, and we commemorate National Day every year, but we must never let the National Day of each year pass casually, nor should we make the National Day of each year become a meaningless ritual. In this National Day commemoration, we should review the lessons, stimuli, and pain we have suffered in the 23-year revolutionary process, and look forward to the arduousness of the national revolution and the work of saving the country and ensuring survival in the future. Everyone should supervise themselves, and should have a new understanding, a new spirit, and new courage. This new understanding, spirit, and courage is to believe in the Three Principles of the People, safeguard national unity, and support a revolutionary leader to save the country and ensure survival. I hope that the citizens of Shanghai can deeply understand this meaning on the occasion of commemorating National Day, take the lead in setting an example, advocate for the whole country, and widely publicize and awaken the people to act in unison. This is the understanding and spirit that we should have in commemorating National Day today." After the speech, he declared the meeting a success and adjourned.

Memorial of Premier's Ordeal in London 101

Municipal Party Department Holds Memorial Meeting

Authorities in the Chinese Concession Strengthen Security

Central News Agency reports that yesterday was the 38th anniversary of Premier's ordeal in London. The Municipal Party Department convened representatives from all walks of life at the auditorium at 10:00 AM to hold a memorial meeting, which was chaired by Tao Baichuan, Executive Committee Member of the Municipal Party Department, who reported on the ordeal and its significance. The Chinese and French military and police authorities have strengthened security. The details of the memorial meeting are as follows:

Representatives Present: Those who attended included Lu Youchang, Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs Supervisory Office, Zhao Zhenhui of the Pharmaceutical Industry Union, Feng Yixian of the Huben Middle School, Lin Kecong of the Women's National Goods Year Movement Committee, Sheng Yizhang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, Zhu Xuefan of the General Labor Union, Yu Yaoqiu of the Southern Goods Industry Union, Yu Zhenhui of the Municipal Farmers' Association, Ma Hanfeng of the Labor Education Association, Pei Yunming of the Land Bureau, Xu Yanrong of the Dyeing Industry Union, He Yuanming and Zhu Yakui of the Jiangsu Fellow Association, Huang Xianggu of the Second Special District Citizens' Federation, Mao Yun of the Law Society, Yu Yuan of the Sixth District Tea Industry Union, Wang Guoping of the Anhui Overseas Students Association, and more than 200 others.

Meeting Order: (1) Opening of the meeting, (2) Singing the Party Song, (3) Paying the highest respect to the Party and National Flags and the Premier's portrait, (4) Reading the Premier's will, (5) Silence, (6) Chairman's report, (7) Speeches, (8) Shouting slogans, (9) Adjournment.

Chairman's Report: After the formalities, Chairman Tao Baichuan delivered a report, briefly stating that, "Today is the 38th anniversary of the Premier's ordeal in London. The Premier once said, 'My knowledge of political life began in that year.' Therefore, the memorial of the ordeal in London occupies an important page in the Premier's revolutionary history. After this, the Premier not only did not have the slightest fear of revolution, but also took the spirit of redoubled efforts to make the revolutionary work more intense and the revolutionary cause more developed. Because of the Premier's spirit of great fearlessness, the revolution has made considerable progress. We are here to commemorate the major setbacks suffered in the process of this revolutionary cause, which makes us more excited about the revolution and how we should strive to complete the unfinished revolutionary work. We believe that the most urgent requirement for the current revolution is that the revolutionary leaders should seek military, political, and economic unification and establish a strong central government. Even if the national crisis is serious, there will be a day to wash away the shame. However, at present, the people of the country are scattered in spirit and expose their lack of organization everywhere. This should awaken the people of the country to thoroughly correct their past mistakes and create a strong Chinese nation."

Memorial Slogans: (1) To commemorate the ordeal in London, we must continue the Premier's spirit of struggle, (2) To commemorate the ordeal in London, we must complete the Premier's unfinished legacy, (3) Eliminate the Red Bandits, (4) Strengthen national power, (5) Strive for production and construction, (6) The Premier's spirit is immortal, (7) Long live the Three Principles of the People.

Grand Opening Ceremony of Two Major Naval Constructions on Double Ten Day 102

Chen Zaofan and Wu Zhennan Each Give Reports

Yixian Warship Enters Dock for Repairs

Central News Agency reports that the new building of the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant and the third dock of the Jiangnan Shipbuilding Plant of the Navy held opening ceremonies on the morning of the day before yesterday (the 10th). Responsible persons from various agencies under the Shanghai Naval Department and guests from all walks of life, totaling more than 500 people, attended, making it a very grand occasion. Russian, French, Belgian, and Italian Consulates Lower Flags to Mourn Death of King of Yugoslavia 106

The Municipal Council Sends Condolences on the Death of the French Foreign Minister

King Alexander of Yugoslavia visited France on the 9th of this month and was assassinated at the same time as French Foreign Minister Barthou. The news came as a shock to all countries. The Russian, French, Belgian, and Italian consulates in this port lowered their flags yesterday morning to mourn the two men.

Due to the death of French Foreign Minister Barthou, Mr. Arnold, the Chairman of the Municipal Council, sent a letter of condolence to the French Consul-General in this port yesterday (11th), expressing deep regret for France's loss of this renowned statesman, and hoping that the other injured would recover their health soon. The Municipal Council office also flew a flag at half-mast yesterday to express condolences.

The Shanghai Evening Post reported that the Chinese government offices in this port lowered their flags today (11th) to mourn the assassination of King Alexander of Yugoslavia in Marseille. The consulates also did the same. Although Soviet Russia was dissatisfied with him because the King was one of the strongest opponents of communism in Europe, its consulate also lowered its flag today. The King usually treated White Russians who took refuge in his country very well, so the White Russians were deeply grateful to him. Since hearing the tragic news, they have been extremely grief-stricken. The charity dance party originally scheduled to be held at Yiyuan yesterday was temporarily cancelled, and a memorial service was scheduled to be held at the Russian church near Alber Road at 7:30 PM tonight, and invitations were sent in advance to Chinese and foreign officials. It is expected that many people will attend. According to reports, the King was also a member of the Russian Orthodox Church.

The Ministry of Finance Issues Certificates for the Intended Boxer Indemnity Loan 110

Principal and Interest Totaling 44,060,000

The Remaining Over 30,000,000 Will Be Issued by the End of October

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, reliable sources in the financial community have confirmed that the Ministry of Finance has been successively issuing "Ping" (Certificate) principal certificates for the Intended Boxer Indemnity Loan, totaling 27,000,000 silver dollars, and "Zheng" (Proof) interest certificates, totaling 17,060,000 silver dollars. The two combined amount to 44,060,000 silver dollars, which are being sent in batches to the loan syndicate and then distributed to the various banks that have undertaken the loan. The remaining 17,000,000 silver dollars in principal certificates and 3,880,000 silver dollars in interest certificates will all be completed and sent to the syndicate before the end of October, which will then distribute them to the banks that have undertaken the loan for their use. It is noted that the total amount of these two types of principal and interest certificates is as high as 64,940,000 silver dollars. Although these certificates are not formally circulated in the market or on exchanges, they are in practice no different from government bonds. In the banking community, their price and credit are considered even higher than all other government bonds and securities, and they can be freely and fully mortgaged or transferred at any time. The certificates can also be used as reserves for issuing banknotes at the Central Bank and as a quarter of the guarantee money for savings banks. This large amount of certificates provides considerable convenience to the banking community by the Ministry of Finance.

Silver Shops Transport Large Quantities of Gold Bars to Hankou 116

Due to Price Decline, Inland Demand is Strong

According to the Xin Sheng News Agency, silver shops in this city have recently been transporting gold to Hankou in very large quantities. The silver shops association has guaranteed to the municipal chamber of commerce that this transportation is for the silver shops' own use and that there is no smuggling involved. The municipal chamber of commerce then guarantees to the customs authorities, and only then can the gold be released. According to an investigation by the municipal chamber of commerce, the reason for the recent increase in gold shipments to Hankou is that various silver shops in this city, such as Lao Fengxiang, Xin Fengxiang, Qing He Fuju, Qing He Faji, and Qiu Tianbao, etc., all have branches in Hankou, Shashi, Yichang, Chongqing, etc. The eighth, ninth, and tenth months of the lunar calendar are the peak season every year, while November to April of the following year is average, and May, June, and July are the off-season. The recent large-scale transport of gold bars to Hankou and other ports is due to the initial price decline and the fact that it is currently the peak season, so the market is broader. If the market price in this city declines further, the demand in the interior will definitely increase, and shipments to various ports along the Yangtze River will become even stronger. If the gold market rises, the inland demand will stagnate, and gold bars may also be transported from the interior to Shanghai.

Death of the Mother of Wang Jingqi 119

The mother of Dr. Wang Jingqi, the former ambassador to Belgium and the Chinese plenipotentiary representative to the International Opium Conference, passed away from illness yesterday, at the age of seventy-eight. Madam Wang had a history of lung disease and relied on the treatment of famous Chinese and Western doctors to stay safe. Unexpectedly, her illness suddenly worsened in recent days. Doctors Huang Cheng, Bomen and Gu Yuqi, Zheng Baoshi and other doctors successively treated her, administering acupuncture and medicine, and there was slight improvement. Eventually, due to her advanced age and weak constitution, she could not be saved and passed away at Shenshi (3-5pm) yesterday. Madam Wang was well-versed in maternal instruction, supported her husband and taught her children, and was known for her virtue. Her children are famous at home and abroad and are praised by the world. When the news of her death came, relatives and friends all mourned her loss. The Shanghai ambassador and his relatives and friends all went to Wang's residence at No. 40 Elmhurst Road to express their condolences. The funeral has been scheduled for the day after tomorrow, and it is expected that the solemn procession will be extremely mournful.
