Grand Opening of the National Child Welfare Leaders Conference Yesterday Morning 121

Speeches by Chairman Kung Hsiang-hsi, Huang Shao-hsiung, Wu Tieh-cheng, and Others

Chiang Kai-shek and Tai Chi-tao Elected as Honorary Chairman and Vice-Chairman

Review Committee Meeting Held in the Afternoon, Plenary Session to Discuss Proposals Today

The National Child Welfare Leaders Conference held its opening ceremony at 9:00 AM yesterday at the New Asia Restaurant Grand Ballroom on Tiantong Road. Exhibits of various forms and products from child welfare associations, nurseries, and orphanages from various provinces and cities were displayed. The grand occasion is described below:

Venue Arrangement: The conference was held in the New Asia Restaurant's Grand Ballroom on the seventh floor. The national flag and the portrait of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen were hung in the center of the hall. The stage was filled with potted flowers. In the center of the stage were seats for the chairman and vice-chairman, with long tables arranged in four rows below. Seats were arranged on both sides, and slogans were hung on the walls: "Child welfare work is the work of cultivating people," "The child welfare conference is a conference for seeking the happiness of children," "The child welfare movement is a movement to save the nation," "The child welfare cause is the cause of nation-building," and so on.

Attending Representatives: More than 170 guests and representatives attended the conference, including Finance Minister Kung Hsiang-hsi, Interior Minister Huang Shao-hsiung, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tieh-cheng, Chairman of the Relief Commission Xu Shi-ying, Wang Xiaolai, Qu Wenliu, Wu Xingya, Wen Hongen, Li Denghui, Lin Kanghou, Tai Xiling, Liu Zhanen, and Du Yuesheng. The ceremony was presided over by Chairman Kung Hsiang-hsi and master of ceremonies Chen Tiesheng.

Opening Remarks by the Chairman: After the ceremony, Chairman Kung Yongzhi, Minister of Finance, gave the opening remarks, saying, "Distinguished guests and representatives, today is the opening of the National Child Welfare Leaders Conference. I am here representing the China Child Welfare Association, and I also welcome you all on behalf of the Association. I am very honored. China's child welfare cause is now widespread throughout the country, and even in the border areas, establishments have been set up. This conference, the National Child Welfare Leaders Conference,"

"does not belong to any individual, nor does it belong to any religion. The Child Welfare Association has been working for six years. In addition to our efforts, we are now moving towards national unification. Therefore, after the establishment of the Child Welfare Association, we wanted to hold a conference for those in the charitable field so that we could all report, exchange opinions, and gain more practical benefits in various aspects, giving child welfare associations everywhere a compass. The foundation of the country depends on the people. The so-called great sages, great men, and great heroes are still individuals, but they have a great relationship with the country and society. For example, Mencius, if he could have been born a sage, then there would have been no need for the education of Mencius' mother. The actions of one person can affect the country and society. Everything in China today, such as education, production, and construction, is backward. God has given us a vast territory and a large nation. We should invigorate ourselves. The past work of the Child Welfare Association has been to cultivate sages, heroes, and the desire to save the country. The child welfare cause is a scientific cause, not only researching but also inventing various things. For example, sometimes people think that children cannot be taught, but some people can educate them to adulthood. The intelligence and wisdom of human beings are different. It is impossible for us to integrate them into one furnace, but our usual method is to teach according to aptitude. What I am contributing to you today is that child welfare is a joint cause. The reason why various causes in China have not been successful is that they are ruined by this. Everyone acts independently, which affects the country and society. If we can unite to educate children in various places and promote parental care in children's families, then I believe that children will serve society in the future with a spirit of cooperation for the country, and we can expect China to become strong. Therefore, the child welfare cause is also a cause of saving the country. Premier Sun Yat-sen once said that the revolution has not yet succeeded, and comrades still need to work hard. Furthermore, in order to achieve the goal of the revolution, he also said to unite with the nations of the world that treat us equally and fight together. If we cannot unite ourselves, how can we unite the world? Today's representatives have come from afar, and I hope that we can exchange opinions on our usual excellent achievements and unite in the future to promote China's child welfare cause." Mayor's Welcome Speech: "Ladies and gentlemen, this year's National Child Welfare Association Leaders Conference is being held in Shanghai. I am very honored to be the host and to gather with child welfare leaders from all over the country. Your association has been established for six years. There are representatives from more than ten provinces participating in your conference today, which shows that your association not only has a long history in time but also a very wide scope in space. In the past six years, the work and achievements that you have made for Chinese society and Chinese children have gradually attracted the attention and sympathy of the people. Therefore, when I welcome you today, I should first express my deep respect for your past efforts. Although child welfare is generally regarded as a social cause, it has become a part of the government's duties due to the evolution of modern countries. Moreover, newborn countries after the war have given constitutional protection to children's lives and rights. Even in ancient China, during periods of clear and bright politics, education and upbringing were always implemented together, and raising children and caring for the elderly were valued by the government. Confucius said, "Let the young be cared for, and the widowed, orphaned, lonely, and disabled be provided for." Mencius said, "Love the young of others as you love your own." These are the important principles of our country's emphasis on child welfare. The importance of the child welfare cause is of course needless for me to elaborate on in front of you. However, in principle of political science, the people are the elements that constitute a country. In principle of sociology and eugenics, the strength of a nation is based on the quality of its people. Therefore, a wise statesman and a visionary entrepreneur pay attention to the education of their citizens. Especially in the process of national revival and strengthening, we should work even harder on this kind of work. The reason why King Goujian of Yue wanted to have ten years of procreation and ten years of training was for this reason. Fichte of Germany was even more specific and practical. He advocated that to revive Germany, we must first start by cultivating the seeds of the nation. In historical fact, the revival of the Yue and the revival of Germany were both the results of this theory. From this ancient and modern Chinese and foreign historical process, we can clearly recognize the connection between the child welfare cause and the revival of the nation. Therefore, I believe that your cause is not a simple social work, but also bears a heavy responsibility for reviving the nation. Regarding this point, I have repeatedly said in the essay contest for your association's Children's Day last year and at the general meeting in the first half of this year. I don't need to repeat it again today. I sincerely wish the development of China's child welfare cause and the success of all of you."

Huang Shao-hsiung's Speech: Next, Interior Minister Huang Shao-hsiung delivered a speech saying, "Chairman, distinguished representatives, the National Child Welfare Leaders Conference is now in session. I am pleased to be able to participate today. Thinking back to the Child Welfare Association, since its establishment in 1928 until now, there have been many achievements in various places. Today, we are gathering child welfare leaders from all over the country to connect with each other. The future benefits will be even greater. In the past in China, we cannot say that there was no child welfare cause, but for various reasons, it could not be expressed. The reason for this is, first, that everyone was doing their own thing. From the people to the government, they could not unite. All of our various causes in China should be done together. Therefore, I hope that the leaders engaged in child welfare can earnestly connect with each other after today's meeting and communicate with the government. Then, when government assistance is needed, the government will certainly assist them. Second, we feel that the past child welfare cause was not in line with scientific organization. The collapse of charitable halls in various places was due to unscientific reasons. I hope that the child welfare cause will be scientific in the future. Then the organization will be sound, the foundation will be solid, and it can forever create happiness for mankind's child welfare. Third, the child welfare cause is of great significance today. The stage from birth to adulthood is worthy of attention. Most children have not received good education and hygiene. How can a new and strong country be created by people who have not received good education and hygiene? Today, countries around the world are paying attention to the education of children because the new country is tied to children. Therefore, our child welfare cause should expand its thinking and work hard on the foundation of the country. Fourth, the gentlemen engaged in child welfare are gathered here today. Next year is Children's Year, and we can come up with a good plan. The Ministry of Interior will provide a large amount of assistance politically," he said.

Congratulations from Wang, Sun, and Tai: (1) Telegram from Premier Wang Zhaoming of the Executive Yuan: "To Vice President Kung, transferred to the full mercy conference for your appraisal, the opening of the conference, Zhaoming is unable to attend due to matters in Beijing, and I am very sorry, I respectfully congratulate the conference on its grand compatriots and the wishes of Kang Ning. "If you can love the young of others as you love your own, then you can make people not only love their own parents but also their own children." Sincerely wish, please share and appreciate." (2) Congratulatory message from Legislative Yuan President Sun Ke: "Spring bamboo sheds its skin, the atmosphere soars to the sky, the clear spring flows newly, gushing like a tide, infants are happily nurtured, their bodies are heroic, their heavenly minds are lively, and kites and fish swim freely. Benevolence and kindness spread widely, and all things and people are compatriots." (3) Ode from Examination Yuan President Dai Jitao: "There are many causes for saving the country, but saving children is the most urgent and effective, and the future holds the greatest hope. Even in terms of management, it is the most enjoyable and meritorious. In all matters under the heavens, good and evil are often opposites. The most meritorious is also the most sinful, the most enjoyable is also the most distressing, and the most beneficial to the country and society is also the most harmful to the country and society. This depends on the heart and actions of those involved. Shakyamuni Buddha taught people to cultivate themselves, saying, "Bodhi is the cause, great compassion is the root, and expediency is the ultimate." He also said, "Wisdom is the mother, and expediency is the father. The Bodhi mind is the mind of great compassion, joy, and equanimity." The meaning of wisdom is most difficult to express. Those without wisdom cannot know what wisdom is. If we try to speculate with foolish opinions, it should be similar to the meaning of "manifesting virtue" in the Great Learning. That is, without the merit and virtue of investigating things, extending knowledge, making intentions sincere, rectifying the heart, cultivating the self, regulating the family, governing the state, and bringing peace to the world, one cannot obtain the clarity of this "manifesting virtue." By analogy, without the merit of giving, observing precepts, patience, diligence, meditation, and wisdom, one cannot achieve the fruit of wisdom. Expediency is everything in everything. People must be able to practice both compassion and wisdom, giving both material and spiritual aid, and then they can speak of expediency. Therefore, this cause of great benefit, great merit, and great joy, if those involved have wisdom and expediency, and their efforts are not beyond their abilities, then the result will easily be the opposite. Therefore, in recent years, I have deeply understood the importance of this cause and have been persuading people to work hard for it every day. I have also tried my best to help others do it, but I have never dared to easily take on the responsibility myself. Is this matter so difficult? I will answer by saying that for someone as foolish and clumsy as I am, I can certainly see that this matter is difficult, truly more difficult than the ancient Shu Road. I dare not use climbing to heaven as an example. Try to think about why there are so many orphaned and suffering children in China. The reason for this is absolutely not in heaven but in people. Also, try to think about why so few young people in China become successful and so many fail to become useful talents. Why is Chinese education less successful and more failing? Why are so few of China's industrial, commercial, agricultural, and forestry enterprises successful and so many unsuccessful? The reason for this is also always due to insufficient human effort. The child welfare cause is related to the family, society, education, and economic enterprise. We dare not say that charitable enterprises can transcend everything and have special achievements. The infant care enterprises in various places can be taken as an example. The proponents of utilitarianism say that only the successful can be considered good under heaven. Although we are unwilling to acknowledge this saying, we also dare not completely oppose it. Therefore, regarding China's charitable enterprise, especially regarding the future of charitable enterprise, we sincerely dare not but be diligent. This is what we earnestly pray of the compassionate leaders, gentlemen, and ladies who are the second parents of the pitiable children."

Madam Tai's Reply: Finally, Ms. Tai Zhizhi, daughter of Madam Tai Xiling, delivered a reply on behalf of her father, saying that her father was ill and asked her to deliver the reply on his behalf. Today, all of you are participating in this conference with enthusiasm for the child welfare cause. I firmly believe that the future of China's child welfare cause will become increasingly prosperous. At the same time, with the support of Finance Minister Kung, the protection of Minister Huang and Mayor Wu, the child welfare cause and those engaged in the child welfare cause will not feel any difficulties politically or economically. What we should strive for is still to make the child welfare cause scientific, and so on. Finally, she thanked the guests who attended the conference on behalf of the conference, and Chairman Kung Hsiang-hsi led all the representatives and guests to take a group photo in the rooftop garden of the New Asia Restaurant as a souvenir.

Election of Conference Staff: After the photography, the participants reconvened in the Grand Ballroom and elected the staff for the conference. Kung Hsiang-hsi was elected as the Chairman of the Conference, Huang Shao-hsiung, Wu Tieh-cheng, Tai Xiling, and Xu Shi-ying as the Vice-Chairmen, Chiang Kai-shek as the Honorary Chairman, Dai Ji-tao as the Honorary Vice-Chairman, Qu Wenliu as the Secretary-General of the Conference, and Zhao Jinqing, Du Yuesheng, and Wang Xiaolai, etc. as the Honorary Executive Directors. After the meeting, the China Child Welfare Association hosted a luncheon at the New Asia Restaurant.

Review Committees: At 3:30 PM, the review committees were convened. The committees included: (Administrative Committee) Ding Shujing, Lin Kanghou, Dai Yangqin, Zhuo Xuanmou, Ge Liting, Sun Weidong, Sheng Guangmao, Wang Kui Sheng, Zhao Xuzhai, Ma Haifeng, Chen Peide, Yuan Zantai, Cao Jiren, Zhou Guangqian, Xu Naili, Zhang Wei, Sun Wang Guoxiu, Li Zhuting, Zhang Xuemen, Shen Erqiao, Zhu Lide, Guan Cuizhen, Tai Zhi, Zhang Dengying, convened by Ding Shujing; (Research Committee) Li Guanfang, Chen Jicheng, Wu Weide, Zeng Nongchun, Dong Renjian, Wan Youzhu, Ma Wenhuan, Wang Wanbai, Hu Shuyi, Liu Zhanen, Yang Weiyu, Xu Yingchang, Su Jielang, Qiu Zitong, Gao Jinglang, Wu Hanzhen, Zhu Youyu, Ying Yuantao, Zhang Wei, Xu Naili, Lai Douyan, convened by Li Guanfang; (Guarantee Committee) Xu Jianping, Lu Bohong, Huang Guibao, Pu Xitai, Cao Mengqi, Wu Weilin, Zhang Zheng Guan, Sun Huizhou, Sang Zhongcheng, Miao Kong, Wu Youlun, Wang Daoyuan, Cai Changqing, Zhu Chonghua, Qian Fugong, Guan Jiongzhi, Xue Weizengpei, Yang Shuping, Lu Ganchen, Wei Xiaofu, Wang Minggao, Tan Jiancheng, Zhu Shaoyang, convened by Xu Jianping; (Relief Committee) Wang Xizhi, Wang Xiaolai, Wu Chong, Li Yaodong, Liang Renjun, Sun Qinglin, Shi Tingdong, Cao Youmo, Xu Xuru, Lu Yigeng, Wang Xianfen, Guo Baoyi, Fu Bulan, Pan Yiran, Zhou Genjing, Huang Zhaibei, Wang Congzhou, Zhu Kaichou, Ye Qinze, Yang Chonggao, Zhang Zhihe, Qin Xiaotao, convened by Wang Xizhi; (Education Committee) Wei Yunyan, Mrs. Guo Shun, Yang Yunying, Wu Wenqing, Wu Yigong, Lu Shuying, Bao Binggong, Cai Shoudao, Peng Wangfen, Li Jingji, Tao Xiaodong, Jiang Xiufeng, Luo Dingchen, Zhou Gen, Bao Fuxian, Li Buqing, Wu Yurui, Shen Yongyan, Li Jingwei, Chen Yiqing, Ye Qingyan, Li Jiahe, Li Laotu, Guo Shouchun, Luo Yunyan, convened by Yang Yunying. The Collapse of the China Industrial Bank 122

Accountant Xu Chao Began Checking Accounts Yesterday

Qunyi Syndicate and Branches Closed Simultaneously

Guowen News Agency reports that the China Industrial Bank at 172 Nanjing Road suddenly announced liquidation yesterday morning due to the manager running away and a financial crisis. Its affiliated China Qunyi Syndicate and six branches were closed simultaneously. The details are recorded below:

Liquidation Notice: Yesterday, lawyer Zhang Ding, representing the Shanghai China Qunyi Syndicate, and accountant Xu Chao, representing the Shanghai China Industrial Bank, issued a liquidation notice stating that, according to the representatives of the aforementioned parties, recently, the manager of the head office, Qin Baoyuan, fled with funds, which occurred suddenly, causing a financial crisis and making it impossible to maintain operations. Effective immediately, liquidation is announced. All creditors are requested to bring their creditor certificates to the office for registration within two weeks of the publication of this notice. Failure to do so will be considered abandonment of the claim. Customers who owe money are also requested to pay directly to this office within the same period, and a receipt will be issued. Failure to do so will result in legal action. (Office: 172 Nanjing Road, 2nd Floor, Telephone 90244) The Bank's History: The bank was established in 1925 during Wu Peifu's powerful reign in Hubei. It was founded by Wu's secretary, Sun Danlin, Gao Enhong, and others, with Zhang Xingsan as the manager. The head office was located in Hankou, with a branch in Shanghai. All remittances from Wu's military and political figures, the Hubei provincial treasury, and Wu's military expenses were paid through the bank. For a time, business was very prosperous. When Wu stepped down, the bank was also affected and reorganized. Xie Jiao Leshan was promoted to manager, and Lu Mengxiang was the co-manager. The head office was moved to Shanghai, and the Hankou head office was changed to a branch. After the September 18th Incident, it was reorganized again, but business was on the verge of danger. Later, Lu Xihou, a standing director, organized the Qunyi Syndicate, invested 300,000 yuan, and mortgaged the bank's own property, the Xingye Lane building on Nanjing Road, for more than 800,000 yuan, which was transferred to the bank, thus enabling it to survive until now.

Branches: In addition to the head office at 172 Nanjing Road, the bank has three other branches in Shanghai: one at 31 Tianzhutang Street, managed by Zhou Shuqing; one at 89 Dongmen Road, Sixteen Puli, Nanshi, managed by Wang Jixuan; and one at 17 Fuxu Road. The Suzhou branch is located on Guanqian Street, and the sub-branch is located on Lindun Road. The Songjiang branch is located on Ximen Street. There was also a branch in Haizhou, but it was closed at the same time as the Hankou branch in August last year. The important personnel of the head office include directors Wu Lihua, Zhang Qingcheng, Tu Baoyi, Ji Zongsu, Zhou Zhufeng, supervisors Yang Kentang, Lu Jingxing, Zhu Junqing, standing director and general manager Xiang Xiang, standing director Lu Xihou, manager Qin Baoguang, and co-manager Lu Mengxiang.

Reasons for Liquidation: According to banking sources, the China Industrial Bank is a limited company, has not joined the Banking Association, and has not issued banknotes. Although it handles savings and remittances, the deposits absorbed in this city are not many, about ten thousand yuan. The reason for the announcement of liquidation is of course that the business is losing money and cannot be maintained.

Female Worker Depositors: After the bank collapsed yesterday, because the newspapers were also in recess, very few people knew about it. It was not until the afternoon that depositors began to register at accountant Xu's office. However, Xu was very busy checking accounts and would have to wait until today or tomorrow to begin registration. When the reporter went to the head office on Nanjing Road in the afternoon, he saw a middle-aged woman standing in front of the bank with her companion. She said that she worked in a light bulb factory and had saved 600 yuan in her lifetime, which she had deposited in the bank to earn interest. Now she unexpectedly announced liquidation. Tears were about to burst from her eyes. Alas!

Formation of Creditor Group: It is reported that the creditors of the bank have formed a creditor group and have engaged lawyer Wang Peiyuan as their agent. The creditor registration office is located at Wang's law office, Room 514, 5th Floor, Continental Market.

Japanese Soldier Stabs Rickshaw Puller 123

Japanese Side Investigating the Culprit

The Continental Daily reports that at around 10:25 PM on Tuesday night, a rickshaw puller from Jiangbei was stabbed in the abdomen with a bayonet by a Japanese Marine soldier of unknown name in a lane near Avenue Doumer. He endured the pain and reported the incident to the nearest patrolman. He was then taken to the Tongren Hospital by rickshaw. It is reported that his injuries are quite critical. According to the rickshaw puller, the soldier hired a rickshaw at the Outer Hongqiao on North Sichuan Road to a dark alley off Avenue Doumer. After getting out of the rickshaw, he only gave the puller ten copper coins. The puller thought it was too little and continued to ask for more. Unexpectedly, the soldier drew his bayonet and stabbed the puller in the abdomen before fleeing. The Avenue du Roi Albert police station, the Japanese consular police, and the Japanese Marines all investigated the assailant. As of late Wednesday night, there were still no clues.

New China Company Apprentice Commits Suicide 125

Two Suicide Notes Expressing Extreme Depression

Lost Future, Unwilling to Live

The Baoshan Hotel on Baoshan Road, Zhabei, had a young lodger check in the afternoon before yesterday. The hotel bookkeeper opened Room 15 for him to stay in. The young man called himself Chen Wangnian, 23 years old, from Yuyao. After slightly consuming tea and water, he closed the door and went to sleep, as if he was exhausted from a long journey. He did not call the tea boy to prepare a meal in the evening. It wasn't until about 8:00 AM yesterday morning that the tea boys suddenly heard moaning coming from the room. Knowing that something had happened, they hurriedly invited the bookkeeper to open the door and enter. They saw that the young man's complexion had changed drastically, and he was barely breathing. They immediately reported to the Beizhan Police Station and sent him to Tongren Hospital for treatment. However, because he had ingested too much poison, it was impossible to save him, and he died in the hospital at about 9:00 AM. Two suicide notes were found on his person, one to his younger brother and one to his uncle and aunt. The general meaning of the notes was that they were full of resentment and dissatisfaction. At the same time, because his job was not satisfactory and the future was uncertain, he took his own life. It was later learned that he had worked as an apprentice at the New China Company at 378 Jiangxi Road before his death. Yesterday afternoon, the corpse was requested to be examined by the local court through the local police, and the local police were ordered to temporarily coffin and bury it, awaiting identification by the relatives of the deceased.

Secret Morphine Smuggling Leaves No Trace; Science Exacerbates Evil 128

Open Smuggling into Shanghai by Boiling Morphine and Soaking it into Wool

Extracting Poisonous Substances from Wool Using Chemical Methods

丨Had There Not Been a Fire, It Would Not Have Been Easily Detected丨

At approximately 10:30 AM the day before yesterday, a massive four-story building at 175, 176, and 177 Aivin Road in Xinzha suddenly caught fire. After the fire was extinguished by the fire brigade, it was discovered by the Xinzha police station that the burned premises was a large-scale morphine manufacturing operation. The details of the morphine manufacturing operation and the aftermath of the fire are described as follows:

Extravagant Lifestyle Cai Bicheng specializes in manufacturing morphine. He lives at No. 24, Lane 1124, Xinzha Road (Qinyuan Village). Having engaged in this business for a long time, his profits are considerable, and his lifestyle is exceptionally luxurious. He owns a private car with license plate number 5787. The morphine manufacturing facility on Aivin Road has been in operation for several months. The building is newly constructed, with a monthly rent of 300 taels of silver. Cai rented it because its location is close to his home, making it easy to manage.

Ingenious Smuggling Method The method of manufacturing morphine is quite novel. The raw materials for morphine all come from Sichuan, but because these are prohibited items, transportation is difficult. Therefore, the raw materials are first boiled in water in Sichuan, and then wool is used to absorb the water. Once the wool is dry, it is packed and transported to Shanghai. As a result, although it is inspected by customs along the way, because the item is wool and has no odor, it has never been discovered. After this wool, saturated with poisonous water, is transported to the manufacturing facility, it is first handed over to the morphine manufacturers on the fourth floor, who re-soak the wool in water, completely washing out the poisonous substances it has absorbed. The clear water immediately turns turbid, and this turbid water is moved to the third floor.

Sudden Fire Alarm On this floor, skilled chemists refine the water, and morphine is finally extracted from the sand. The cost of the raw materials is very low, and the refined morphine is sold at a high price. At noon the day before yesterday, the third floor was in the process of chemical refining when an engineer carelessly allowed chemical liquid to come into contact with fire, causing the fire. All those working on the third floor, seeing the intense flames and being unable to extinguish them, fled together, hurriedly rushing to Cai Bicheng's residence to report. Cai, realizing that the secret would inevitably be exposed, drove away in his private car after hearing the alarm, ordering his driver, Xu Laisheng, to flee quickly.

Two Arrested At this time, the fire brigade and the Xinzha police station each sent personnel to rush to the fire scene. They all noticed a strange smell emanating from the smoke. Initially, they suspected that opium was being burned. After the fire was extinguished, they suddenly saw two people escaping from the roof of the fourth floor to a neighboring house. They were intercepted by Detective Tang Jian, Detective Lu Gendi, and Detective Yang Youshan, who were at the scene. They immediately entered the burning house to investigate and learned that it was a morphine manufacturing operation. The manufacturing equipment on the third and fourth floors was still intact, and there were many remaining raw materials. According to those familiar with the morphine market, the value of the morphine that had been manufactured and not yet manufactured in the house was considerable.

Principal Offender at Large Detective Tang and others, seeing the numerous items in the house, took the two arrested men back to the police station for questioning. They learned that one was Gong Baochang from Tongzhou, and the other was Miao Zhangcai from Anhui, both of whom worked on the fourth floor. The police chief ordered them to be detained and dispatched many Chinese and foreign detectives to guard the morphine manufacturing facility. Meanwhile, Detective Tang and others were sent to Cai Bicheng's home to arrest the principal offender. However, Cai had already driven away in his car. Therefore, all police stations were notified to be on alert. Soon, Cai's car was discovered in the garage of a Mr. Qiu at No. 21 Xieqiao Road. Qiu was a friend of Cai's. Cai drove out of his house and, passing Qiu's garage, abandoned the car and fled. His driver then temporarily parked the car there.

Judicial Inspection Soon after, the gatekeeper of the Commercial Press workshop, which was near the manufacturing facility, also arrested Gong Wenfu, a worker from Tongzhou, who had fled from the fourth floor. All of them were sent to the First Special District District Court yesterday morning. Judge Liu Yugui conducted the interrogation. The police lawyer Zhang Tianyin briefly described the situation and requested a site inspection. Judge Liu questioned Gong and the other two men, who all stated that they had recently been hired and received a monthly salary of eight yuan. Judge Liu ordered them to be detained and scheduled to personally inspect the fire scene at 2:30 PM today.

The Women's National Goods Year Committee Visits the National Goods Cosmetics Exhibition 131

In this era of industrial decline and commercial recession, the Family Industry Cooperative is uniquely able to cope with ease. It is estimated that the business volume for the nine months of this year has exceeded the total for the entire year of last year by more than one time. It is only through excellent products and proper management that this can be achieved. By around 2:00 PM, even the pedestrians on the road were blocked. The Family Industry Cooperative contacted the Public Works Department by telephone to request additional police to maintain order. Meanwhile, a temporary universal coupon was issued. Anyone holding this coupon would receive the same treatment as on Double Ten Day for purchases made from the Family Industry Cooperative within ten days. The exhibition period for the Inter-Aid National Goods Cosmetics Industry Exhibition was extended for ten days. Those without coupons were not eligible. The cooperative's manager, Chen Xiaodie, personally oversaw the proceedings at the scene. Purchasers entered and exited the Family Industry Cooperative sales department in an orderly manner. The guests were able to freely select and purchase to their satisfaction. According to Mr. Chen, mutual assistance among industries is the newest element in modern commerce, and this is not limited to the cosmetics industry. Therefore, there are plans to expand it and rename it the National Goods Treasures Association. All related industries with connections to household daily necessities can gather for exhibition. The Family Industry Cooperative will provide commercial space and be responsible for advertising and promotional expenses, to achieve the justice of industry association. It is said that after the cosmetics exhibition closes, the knitting industry will continue the exhibition. The knitting industry association has already contacted the Family Industry Cooperative.

Distribution of various designs for the new family life

There is another rest area, occupying a house, displaying various photos of Xinhua Bank and various savings trust charts and meaningful models, showing the bank's service to all aspects of society. In addition, there are several open spaces that are being designed and constructed, with land demarcation and tree planting, which is extremely busy. It can be seen that the village is developing rapidly, and it is indeed an unprecedented achievement in creating a new village in the city. The village occupies a rectangular area of more than 50 acres and is divided into more than 40 houses, divided into five types: A, B, C, D, and E. The architectural styles are different from each other. The value, including land and construction equipment, ranges from 3,400 yuan to 20,000 yuan. Subscribers can first pay three-tenths of the full price, and the rest can be repaid in installments. It is most economical for middle-class citizens. It is now estimated that two-thirds of all houses have been subscribed for. Moreover, the location is moderate, the scenery is quiet, the transportation is convenient, the public utility facilities are complete, and the surrounding security is complete, which meets the conditions of an ideal residence. The weather was sunny yesterday, and more than 3,000 visitors came, including ladies and gentlemen. Many groups and schools went there in groups. For a time, the carriages and horses were bustling, which was really a grand occasion. At that time, Xinhua Bank also distributed small booklets of various living application designs for the new family, one for each person, to add to the fun, which is also one of the bank's services to the community.

New Business Path of Ningbo Industrial Bank 135

Since moving to its new location, the business of Ningbo Industrial Bank has been extremely developed. It is now known that the bank has signed a special agreement with Shanghai National Goods Company and China National Goods Production and Sales Company for national goods revolving collateral loans to assist various factories. A national goods market has been established on the second floor of the bank to promote national goods. The bank's business has opened up a new path, and the future of national goods is greatly beneficial. The bank's national goods revolving collateral loan regulations are listed on the left: "In order to support national goods industries and commerce and facilitate production and sales cooperation, the bank has specially established a type of national goods revolving collateral loan, and the method is as follows: 1. Pure Chinese national goods can be used to borrow funds from the bank. The goods used as collateral can still be freely sold with the bank's consent, which is called national goods revolving collateral loan. 2. All goods used as collateral must be those that are commonly sold on the market, and their value must be based on the current market price. 3. The discount on the collateral loan will be determined based on the rise and fall of the goods value. If the market price falls, the collateral borrower should increase the collateral items. The collateral loan interest and term will be negotiated bilaterally. 5. If Shanghai National Goods Company or China National Goods Production and Sales Company is entrusted to act as a wholesale agent for sales, Shanghai National Goods Company will issue a proof of inventory, and the proof of inventory can be used as collateral for this collateral loan. 6. The remaining goods stored in the company that have not been sold should be redeemed by the collateral borrower within a time limit. If a continued loan is required, it will be determined by the bank. 7. All collateral loans must be insured, and the insurance policy must be deposited with the bank and transferred to the bank's name. 8. All revolving collateral loans must find a reliable guarantor. 9. If the goods cannot be sold out upon expiration and the collateral borrower cannot redeem them, the bank has the right to auction them freely. The collateral borrower voluntarily waives the right to first prosecution defense, and if the auction is insufficient, the guarantor shall be responsible for repaying the principal and interest. 10. The bank may revise these regulations at any time.

Rice Industry Elder Gong Zhaoming Passes Away 138

Gong Zhaoming, a senior figure in the rice industry, has been engaged in the rice business in Shanghai for more than 40 years. As the general manager of Yuchang Rice Shop, his business has flourished and is the best in Shanghai. He has served as a director of the Jiagutang Rice Industry Association, an executive committee member of the Shanghai Rice Shop Industry Association, and an executive committee member of the Jiangsu Ninghu Municipal and County Rice Industry Federation. He has made many plans for the reform of the industry and has been fair and just, resolving difficulties and disputes. He has been admired by the industry. Since last year, due to overwork, he has suffered from numbness. He was treated by famous Chinese and Western doctors, but all were ineffective. This summer, he returned to his hometown of Nanhui to recuperate, and passed away on the 8th of this month, at the age of 61. Those in the industry who heard about it were all saddened.

Lawyer Zhu Kuangming Sues Lawyer Gu Jirong Case 139

Re-examined by Judge Wu Tingqi

Witness Li Huchen testified in court yesterday

Lawyer Gu Jirong was previously commissioned by Tao Shangen to sue Pan and others for debt disputes. After the First Special District District Court ruled that the defendants should repay the debt, Pan and others refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the second and third instance courts by their lawyer Zhu Kuangming. However, the results were all unsuccessful, and Pan was afraid of being executed, so he fled to the Chinese Concession. Recently, he was still arrested by the Shanghai Local Court in the city in order to be escorted and pursued. At this time, Tao Shangen suddenly received a letter from the debtor, stating that the previous second and third instance appeals were not their intention. Tao's friend was by his side, and upon reading this letter, he stated that since it was not Pan and others who insisted on appealing, it must have been Pan and others' lawyer Zhu Kuangming who acted without authorization. Therefore, he encouraged Tao to file a criminal private prosecution with the Shanghai Local Court against Zhu, accusing him of forging documents. Unexpectedly, while Tao was involved in a lawsuit with Zhu, he also discussed with his lawyer Gu Jirong and Ji Chao, who had previously served as Gu's clerk. First, he notified Zhu Kuangming by telephone, requesting a private settlement outside. Then, he personally went to Zhu's office to discuss the settlement terms, and said that the local court had issued an arrest warrant, and if he could pay 500 yuan, the case could be closed. Gu drafted a settlement draft. Zhu, seeing that they were intent on extortion and could not be reasoned with, immediately detained the draft and reported it to the police. Gu Jirong and Tao Shangen then separately left Zhu's residence. Zhu then filed a complaint with the First Special Court accusing Gu, Tao, and Ji Chao of colluding in fraud. The summons of the various parties has been reported in detail in this newspaper. It is now known that the case should be tried by Judge Wu Tingqi, but Wu was ill and requested leave to recuperate. Therefore, Judge Zhan Liangce tried the case. Now that Judge Wu has recovered from his illness and has returned to the court to work as usual, the case is still being handled by Judge Wu. Yesterday afternoon, he specially summoned the original defendant, the plaintiff, and both parties' witnesses to the court for a new trial. However, the disputes and events described by the original plaintiff and the defendant were the same as the previous statements, so there is no need to repeat them. Afterwards, witness Li Huchen was summoned to the court for questioning. Li stated that he was a clerk in Lawyer Gao's office and was a neighbor of Lawyer Zhu. On August 23rd, Gu Jirong and Tao Shangen went to Zhu's office. Afterwards, they asked Zhu to return the draft, but Zhu refused to return it, so they quarreled. Witness Zhang Dingxiang testified that on August 9th, I went to Zhu's office. Ji Chao was also present and said that Gu Jirong had ordered him to come to Zhu to negotiate a settlement of the case, and Ji also wanted Zhu to pay some money. However, the defendant Ji Chao denied going to Zhu's office, saying that Zhu called me to mediate, and cited Qin Xing to testify. Judge Wu ordered a change of date for another hearing because further investigation was needed.

Robbery in Wufu Lane 140

At about 6:30 AM yesterday morning, the home of Rong Shuxin, a butcher, at No. 39 Wufu Lane, Nanjing Road, was suddenly broken into by three robbers. Man Collapses and Dies on Zhongxing Road 141

At 8:30 AM yesterday morning, at the intersection of Zhongxing Road and Hongxing Road in Zhabei, a man in his forties, wearing a blue cloth shirt and trousers, suddenly fell ill, collapsed to the ground, and died. Passers-by reported the incident to Liang Fuchu, Director of the North Station Branch of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who immediately sent Patrol Officer Jia Wenbin to the address to investigate and learned that the deceased was Lu Shaoyun, a native of Anhui, 47 years old, a tea worker. He had previously suffered from heart pain. Yesterday morning, he suddenly relapsed, worsened, and died. However, the deceased had no family members, only an uncle. After receiving the report, Director Liang instructed the local bail to report to the local court to send someone to examine the body.

Horse Mouxiang, a Former Detective, Commits Multiple Crimes 142

Sentenced to Six Months Imprisonment After Interrogation

Ma Mouxiang, a Henan native and former detective No. 5 of the General Inspectorate, was arrested and sent to the First Special Court on suspicion of inciting injury. The initial trial resulted in Ma being declared innocent. Subsequently, the Inspectorate appealed, and the Second High Court of Appeals concluded the trial, overturning the original verdict and sentencing Ma to eight months' imprisonment. However, Ma had been released on bail during the appeal and fled without a trace upon hearing the sentence, avoiding arrest. Later, the Special Court offered a reward of 500 yuan for his capture. On the 5th of this month, detectives from the Chinese Public Security Bureau apprehended Ma and handed him over to the Special Court for imprisonment. Now, Yang Chengjie, a Chinese detective from the Putuo Road Inspectorate, has discovered that Ma, while serving as a detective last March, had a thief steal a pair of binoculars and pawn them at Hongde Pawnshop on Father Jin's Road. Ma, as a detective, went to the pawnshop to identify the original thief. The victim redeemed the pawn for 15 yuan, which Ma embezzled for his own use, issuing a receipt to the pawnshop for record, but never paid the victim. Similarly, he embezzled the pawn money of 10 yuan for a typewriter from Qingyuan Pawnshop on Hankou Road, 22 yuan for a coat from Changsheng Pawnshop on Beihai Road, and 12 yuan for clothes from Tongyuan Pawnshop on Baker Road. After reporting these multiple cases to the head of the Inspectorate, Ma was brought from prison and sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court yesterday morning. Zhang Tianyin, the Inspectorate's lawyer, presented the case, prosecuting Ma for embezzlement in the course of his duties under Article 357 of the Criminal Law. After clear interrogation by Judge Liu, Ma Mouxiang was sentenced to six months' imprisonment for continuous embezzlement in the course of his duties, to be served concurrently.

Illicit Morphine Trafficker Sentenced to One Year 143

Zhang Renlin, a native of Tongzhou, was recently found to be secretly selling the drug morphine for profit inside house number 7, Lane Yihe, Huaji Road. Qian Peijin, a detective from the Huishan Inspectorate, discovered this a few days ago and rushed to the address for arrest. Finding the door tightly closed, he peered through the crack and saw Zhang packaging morphine in paper. He forced the door open and entered, and Zhang surrendered. He was taken to the Inspectorate along with fourteen small packets of morphine, a vial of liquid, and a needle, and was detained. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Li Zhishan, the lawyer of the Public Works Department, recounted the previous events, stating that the defendant was a fugitive and requesting strict punishment. When questioned, Zhang gave evasive answers. Judge Xiao sentenced Zhang Renlin to one year's imprisonment as a warning, and the evidence was confiscated.

Young Man Attempts Suicide in Hotel 144

At approximately 8 p.m. the night before last, a young man arrived at the Zhongnan Hotel at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Changsha Road, carrying a suitcase, and checked in. He identified himself as Zhao Changyu, 22 years old, from Ningbo. The hotel clerk led him to room number 8. After having some tea, he went out and did not return until midnight, when he closed the door and went to sleep. However, he had not gotten up by noon yesterday. The tea server became suspicious and opened the door to check, finding Zhao lying stiffly in bed, his face pale, and unconscious. Empty bottles of sleeping pills were found under the bed and on the table. Realizing he had taken poison, they immediately reported it to the Inspectorate, which dispatched a vehicle to rush him to Renji Hospital for treatment. However, due to the strength of the drug, despite emergency treatment, he remains unconscious and in critical condition.

Bank Inspection Report Summary 153

The Central Bank issued its 210th Examination Report on Issuance Preparation: This association is responsible for inspecting the Central Bank's issuance of convertible currency reserves in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Ordinance. The 210th inspection was carried out at the Bank's Issuing Bureau on October 9, 1934, and the results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible currency issued is 81,164,366 silver dollars, including 74,852,172 silver dollar notes and 6,312,194 fractional currency notes. The total amount of convertible currency reserves is 81,164,366 silver dollars, including 65,610,366 silver dollars in cash reserves. This cash reserve includes 62,060,998 yuan deposited in the Bank's issuing vault, 1,700,249 yuan deposited in branches in various ports, and 1,848,119 yuan deposited with fellow banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 15,554,000 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible currency issued is 373,324.7 yuan. The total amount of customs gold convertible currency reserve is 373,324.7 yuan. This reserve includes 7,351.95 taels of standard gold, which is converted to 373,324.7 customs gold at a fixed price of .50779. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Currency Regulations, 60% of the cash reserve and 40% of the guarantee reserve. The result of this inspection is that the amount of cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. October 11, 1934, Li Fukun, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Supervisors Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Qi.

The Four Banks Reserve Depository is jointly established by the Yanyeh, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Dalu Banks to exclusively handle the issuance of Zhongnan Bank notes. According to the Depository's issuance regulations, the issuance of banknotes is fully reserved, with a cash reserve of at least 60% and a guarantee reserve of at most 40%. It is announced once a week, and inspected by the auditors and chief accountants of the four banks. The 49th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Depository on October 6, 1934, is recorded as follows: The amount of banknotes in circulation is 27,146,387 yuan. The total amount of reserves is 27,146,387 yuan, including a cash reserve of 21,318,087 yuan and a guarantee reserve of 5,828,300 yuan.

Sports News

North China Games Opens on Double Tenth Day 157

Two National Records Broken

Wu Bixian High Jumps 1.83 Meters

Tan Fuzhen 400m Hurdles in 59 Seconds

(Tianjin, 11th) The 18th North China Games opened on the Double Tenth Day at the newly built Tianjin Stadium. First, a ceremony was held for the completion of the venue, followed by the opening ceremony of the Games. Important figures from China and abroad participated in the grand ceremony. The Double Tenth Day featured many ball games, and today's focus was on track and field events. The weather was sunny and pleasant, and the audience was very enthusiastic and lively. Many North China records were broken in track and field. Wu Bixian broke the national record in the men's high jump with a height of 1.83 meters, and Tan Fuzhen broke the national record in the 400m hurdles with a time of 59 seconds. The details are as follows:

Completion Ceremony of the Venue 158

(Tianjin, 10th) The completion ceremony of the venue was originally scheduled to be held at 7:00 a.m., but was delayed until 8:40 a.m. Chairman Yu Xuezhong reported on the significance of the construction of the venue. Wang Zhengting gave a political speech on behalf of the guests, saying that after the construction of the Hebei Stadium, there are two hopes for the athletes: (1) to exercise their bodies and become useful citizens, and (2) to cultivate the spirit of cooperation and unity in preparation. Then, Yu Xuezhong's wife, Zhang Xuehui, cut the rope, released training pigeons, and the music ended.

Opening Ceremony of the Games 159

(Tianjin, 10th) The opening ceremony of the 18th North China Games was held at 9:15 a.m. this morning after the completion of the venue. Everything proceeded in order as follows. Yu Xuezhong gave a report, expecting the athletes to uphold the spirit of sports, not forgetting national humiliation and being brave, paying attention to universal love, unity, and martial arts. Then, Vice President Zhou Bingqi of the Hebei Department of Education, Gan Shi of the North China Preparatory Committee, Yuan Dunli, Chief Referee Zhang Boling, Ma Yuehan, representative of the North China Sports Federation, Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, Hao Gengsheng, representative of the Ministry of Education, and He Qigong, representative of the Political and Rectification Committee, gave speeches in succession. The ceremony ended at 10:15 a.m. The flag was raised and the music was played, and the audience and all members of the Games stood in solemn silence. Eighteen cannons were fired.

Athlete's Parade (Tianjin, 10th) Athletes from each unit entered the arena at 8:00 a.m., led by military music. The order was: Cha, Qingdao, Lu, Jin, Shan, Shaan, Liao, Ji, Hei, Re, Ha, Ping, Yu, and Ji. There were 881 male athletes and 228 female athletes, who circled the arena and gathered in front of the podium. The Ping and Ji athletes were the most lively, and the Lu and Jin athletes were the most simple. The announcer of the Games proceeded according to the program, and the ceremony was as usual.

Foreign Guests Present (Tianjin, 10th) The foreign guests present today included the U.S. Consul in Tianjin, the U.S. Commander, the British Army Commander. From the Japanese side, in addition to the Commander of the Garrison Army, Meizu, and his staff, Aoki and Kawaguchi, there were also Consul Tanaka, Police Chief Wakyui, and Adjutant Oie of the Garrison Army. They paid special attention to the speeches of our important figures and the spirit and discipline of the athletes.

Male and Female Students' Exercises (Tianjin, 10th) At 10:30 a.m. on the 10th, various performances began. First, all elementary school students performed Tai Chi, with approximately 600 participants, all wearing white uniforms, neat and lively. Tens of thousands of spectators in the audience applauded. The second performance was a "Riding the Wind and Breaking the Waves" dance by more than 500 female students. The third performance was a knife-wielding performance by the Public Security Bureau's security team, and flag signals by the elementary school Boy Scouts, all of which were orderly and solemn. The most exciting was the bayonet drill by the security team. The flashing knives and the loud battle cries added a lot of color to the Games. The morning program ended at 11:30 a.m.

Men's High School Track and Field Report 160

Long Jump (Tianjin, 11th) Men's High School Long Jump Final: (1) Wang Shilin (tie), (2) Hong Yiting (Qingdao), (3) Liu Mengling (Qingdao), (4) Zhang Lingjia (tie). The result was 6.51 meters. The second place was 6.49 meters, which was very close to the first place. Hong Yiting is a veteran jumper from Guanghua University in Shanghai, and has a previous record of 6.75 meters. Because the ground was soft and difficult to exert force, he only achieved this result on his sixth jump.

American Track and Field Team's Visit to Shanghai, Association Invites Performance 172

Expected within this month

The American track and field team has already set off eastward to visit the Philippines and Japan. Shanghai is a necessary stop for the team. The Association authorities plan to take advantage of their passage and invite them to land and perform, so that people in our country can observe and learn. They have already contacted Mr. Topping, the secretary of the Western Qiao Youth Association, for consultation. It is learned that when the team returns from the Philippines and passes through Shanghai (around the end of the month), it will be the opening of the International Games, and they will perform on stage.

National Day Football Match: Tung Wah Defeats Holders 173

Tung Wah Concedes First Goal

Wins 2-1 in the End

After returning from their northern expedition, the Tung Wah football team specially arranged a friendly match against the Holders team during the National Day holiday at Shen Yuan. Tung Wah, with the addition of Gu Shangxiang and the return of Chen Jiaqiu, seemed stronger than before. However, Lu Zhong'en's goalkeeping showed considerable nervousness, and Feng Yunyou's prowess had diminished compared to the past. The midfielders and forwards were all good. Wan Xianghua did not play on this day. The first half ended scoreless. In the second half, after Tung Wah conceded a goal due to a careless mistake by goalkeeper Lu, they relied on Dai Linjing and Li Yichen's final efforts to win 2-1. The audience was very enthusiastic, making it the first grand occasion of the new autumn football season.

Holders kicked off and took an early lead, surprising Tung Wah. Tung Wah launched fierce attacks on the opponent's goal. The forwards' short passes were beautiful and their attacks were swift, drawing cheers from the audience. Li Yichen made a header and a shot, and Feng Yunyou made a long-range attack, although they did not score, they won the approval of the whole stadium and gave the opponents a scare. After about ten minutes, the Holders broke free and a forward penetrated Tung Wah's defenses from the right, disturbing Tung Wah's flanks. Mao Lin charged left and right in front of the goal, trying to score but failing, thanks to the defensive efforts of Li Ning and Guan Xun'an.

The Holders attacked again from the right wing, with Curtis sprinting and sending a high ball to the front of the goal. Mao Lin headed the ball to the front, and A Qiao used lightning-fast speed to head the ball as well. Fortunately, Lu was quick-eyed and quick-handed, catching the ball and averting the danger. The ball flowed back and forth in the field like a meteor, and the pace was fast-paced and the situation was quite tense. Both sides' midfielders had solid defenses that were difficult to break through quickly. Lu Zhong'en's goalkeeping, however, showed considerable nervousness, causing spectators to sweat.

Chen Hongguang threw the ball from the sideline, and the ball bounced back from Jiaqiu's head. Hongguang kicked the ball long towards the opponent's goal. Dai Linjing, being marked by the opponent, cleverly lobbed the ball high, and Yichen immediately ran up and headed it, but unfortunately it bounced off the crossbar. Qiu Ting rushed up to attack again but was stopped by the goalkeeper. Zhou Guangzhong kicked a high ball from the left, unintentionally creating an excellent opportunity, as the ball landed right in front of the goal, but it was saved by Herbert. After half an hour, A Qiao got the ball on the left wing and broke through Tung Wah's defense, reaching the goalmouth. At this critical moment, Li Ning rushed up from the side and tackled A Qiao, and Lu Zhong'en seized the opportunity to grab the ball and escape danger.

The first half passed uneventfully. At the start of the second half, both sides made changes to their lineups. Zhou Guangzhong was replaced by Cao Qiuting on Tung Wah's left wing. Jia Youliang replaced the right wing. The Holders also replaced Curtis on the right wing with the mediocre Li Queshi, greatly reducing their strength. Dai Linjing made a solo run, attacking the opponent's goal from an oblique angle. Unexpectedly, the ball went straight at the goalkeeper, who caught it safely. Yichen showed off his skills, dribbling left and right in front of the opponent's goal, trying to find an opportunity to score, but the opponent's marking was very tight, and there was no gap to exploit. The performance of both sides was not as good as before, and the formations were loose and spiritless.

As the game dragged on, a sudden change occurred, like a stimulant for a patient. The Holders took two consecutive corner kicks from the right wing, causing Tung Wah a scare. Tao Lewei sent the ball from the center to the right wing, then back to the front of the goal. At this time, Tung Wah's midfield formation was chaotic, and Mao Lin took the opportunity to shoot, but the ball was weak. Lu Zhong'en dived to catch the ball but was slow, and A Qiao rushed up and pushed the ball into the net, giving them the lead. The spectators were stunned and laughed.

After misfortune comes good fortune, and fortune and misfortune are unpredictable. Had Tung Wah not conceded this goal, perhaps they would not have been motivated to attack. Therefore, after this mistake, Tung Wah rallied and won 2-1. Tung Wah kicked off from the center and launched an attack. Within three minutes, Jiaqiu received a high ball from Yichen from the sideline and passed it to Linjing. Dai kicked hard at the goal, catching the opponent off guard. The ball grazed goalkeeper Herbert and went into the net, tying the score. After a long period of maneuvering, as time was about to run out, Li Yichen made a solo run, shooting obliquely from the right corner. The ball was fast and went straight into the corner of the net. Herbert could not save it, and Tung Wah scored another goal, winning 2-1. The lineups were as follows:

Tung Wah Association

Lu Zhong'en Guan Xun'an Li Ning Chen Hongguang Feng Yunyou Gu Shangxiang Jia Youliang (replaced by) Cao Qiuting Chen Jiaqiu Dai Linjing Li Yichen Zhou Guangzhong (replaced by) Cao Qiuting

China International Library Hosts World Library Exhibition 178

Opening Ceremony on Double Tenth Day, Wu Zhihui Delivers Opening Speech

Participants Include 66 Libraries from 16 Countries

Exhibition to Last One Week, Closing on the 16th of This Month

The World Library Exhibition organized by the China International Library opened on Double Tenth Day at 393 Ferguson Road. The opening ceremony was presided over by Wu Zhihui, the founder of the library. 66 renowned libraries from 16 countries are participating. The exhibition will last one week and is scheduled to close on the 16th of this month. Details are as follows:

Participating Countries: The countries participating in the exhibition include Germany, Britain, Austria, Canada, Denmark, Spain, the United States, France, the Netherlands, Ireland, Italy, Poland, Romania, Sweden, Switzerland, and China, for a total of 16 countries.

International Participants: The participants include the German National Library of Berlin, the University Library of Hamburg, the University Library of Jena, the State and University Library of Königsberg, the Stuttgart Library, the Bristol Public Library of Britain, the Library of Congress, the London Library, the Vienna Library of Austria, the University Library of Innsbruck, the Toronto Public Library of Canada, the Aarhus Library of Denmark, the University Library of Copenhagen, the Esbjerg Library, the Catalonia Library of Spain, the Chicago Library Association of the United States, the Boston Public Library, the Library of Congress, the Pratt Institute Free Library of New York, the National Library of Paris of France, the Versailles Library, the Soissons Library, the Paris Chamber of Commerce Library, the University Library of Amsterdam of the Netherlands, the Delft University of Technology Library, the Amsterdam Colonial College Library, the Patent Office Library, the Rotterdam Library, the Hague Library, the Karolinska University Library, the Dublin Library of Ireland, the National Library of Naples of Italy, the University Library of Naples, the University Library of Genoa, the Archiginnasio Municipal Library of Poland, the University Library of Cluj of Romania, the Academy Library, the Lund University Library of Sweden, the Bern Library of Switzerland, the Geneva Public Library, the Basel University Library, and the Zurich Central Library, totaling 42 institutions.

Domestic Participants: The participants include the China International Library of Geneva, the Library of the Ministry of Railways of Nanjing, the National Central University Library of Nanjing, the Tongji University Library of Shanghai, the First Provincial Library of Hebei, the National Central Library, the National Peiping Normal University Library, the Sino-French University Library of Peiping, the Jiangsu Provincial National Studies Library, the Shandong Provincial Library, the National Tsinghua University Library of Peiping, the Yenching University Library of Peiping, the National Palace Museum of Peiping, the Guangzhou University Library, the Jinan University Library, the St. John's University Library, the National Library of Peiping, the First Municipal Library of Peiping, the Shandong Provincial Library, the Shanghai Municipal Library, the University of Nanking Library, the Zhejiang Provincial Library, the Anhui Provincial Library, the Fujian Provincial Library, the Guangdong National University Library, the Fuzhou Wushan Library, and the Wuchang Boone Library School, totaling 24 institutions.

Exhibition Arrangement: The exhibition venue is the World Society Auditorium at 393 Ferguson Road. The walls and center are filled with exhibits such as photographs, charts, publications, etc., totaling more than 1,200 items. The arrangement is quite exquisite. Among the libraries of various countries, the Austrian National Library of Vienna, the German National Library of Berlin, and the Library of Congress of the United States are the most grand in scale and luxurious in architecture, ranking first in the world. The National Central Library of China is displaying a reprint of the Siku Quanshu published by the Commercial Press, which is particularly impressive.

Opening Ceremony: The opening ceremony was held at 3:00 PM on Double Tenth Day. More than 100 people attended, including the founder of the library, Wu Zhihui, the director, Feng Chen Zuyi, Li Dachao of the municipal government, Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau, President Liu Zhanen of Shanghai University, Zhu Shaoping of the World Student Association, Xu Zexiang, director of the Municipal Library, Du Dingyou, director of the Jiaotong University Library, Xu Zongze, director of the Xujiahui Library, Lin Jun of the French Literary Society, and artists Sun Fuxi and Hua Lin. The ceremony began with an opening speech by Wu Zhihui, followed by a report on the preparation process by Feng Chen Zuyi. Finally, Director Pan, Du Dingyou, Xu Zongze, and others delivered speeches before the ceremony concluded.
